mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">母志太</span></b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">四川绵阳市法轮功学员。</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">男，<span lang="EN-US">1969</span>年生，四川绵阳市北川县人，<span lang="EN-US">1997</span>年开始修炼法轮功。</span><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">1999</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，中共邪党开始迫害法轮功后，他多次被抓捕、关押，曾两次被劳教、<span lang="EN-US">1</span>次被判刑。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日晚，母志太被绵阳市涪城区公安警察抓捕。涪城区公安警察抄了他儿子的房屋和他自己的租房屋，抢走很多私人财产。母志太被关押在绵阳市看守所近半年。绵阳市涪城区法院在<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日对母志太庭审。律师在法庭上为母志太做了无罪辩护。未当庭宣判。后得知其被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/19/%E5%9B%9B%E5%B7%9D%E7%BB%B5%E9%98%B3%E5%B8%82%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E6%AF%8D%E5%BF%97%E5%A4%AA%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4-441460.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span color="windowtext" face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/19/%E5%9B%9B%E5%B7%9D%E7%BB%B5%E9%98%B3%E5%B8%82%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E6%AF%8D%E5%BF%97%E5%A4%AA%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4-441460.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">慕恩：</span></b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">安徽合肥基督教青年团契带领同工，<span lang="EN-US">1988</span>年生，男，已婚，有一女<span lang="EN-US">8</span>岁一子<span lang="EN-US">6</span>岁，与父母同住。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，“合肥青年团契”在聚会时被冲击，<span lang="EN-US">84</span>人当场被抓捕，警方押着王以诺到家里搜查，搜了几个小时，并没有搜查令也没有拘捕令，就把人抓走了。当天被抓的多数人<span lang="EN-US">24</span>小时之后释放，有<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人关押<span lang="EN-US">7</span>天后释放。被释放的人后来都没有什么事。主要同工王以诺、慕恩被刑拘，后被批准逮捕。家属在<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月份收到通知，<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日开庭。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月获悉慕恩被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚款<span lang="EN-US">6</span>万元；王以诺弟兄被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">5</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/06/363.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span color="windowtext" face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/06/363.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">木拉提别克•吾麻尔：</span></b><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">1984</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年出生，新疆伊犁哈萨克自治州（简称伊犁州）巩留县人，哈萨克族公民，穆斯林，伊犁州<span lang="EN-US">/</span>巩留县<span lang="EN-US">/</span>吉尔格郎乡<span lang="EN-US">/</span>阿勒玛勒村清真寺教长（又称伊玛目）助手（经国家对宗教人士资格认证），中国在押良心犯。自<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年起，因中共政府对新疆地区各少数族裔施行更严酷的高压管控政策，遂中共新疆当局开始大规模抓捕维吾尔族、哈萨克斯坦族穆斯林，清除所有带有少数民族文化特征的标志、广告牌及食品等，收缴或焚烧《古兰经》，并将数以万计的穆斯林强送“职业技能教育培训中心”（实为培训转化集中营）接受汉化教育；对于少数民族的各种聚会（尤以举行相关宗教敬拜、祷告仪式等为甚），更是设法取；后在国际社会关注下，从<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年初开始，中共当局才被迫将一部分在押培训者予以释放，但同时，又将另一部分人予以秘密重判入狱；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，其因与所在阿勒玛勒村清真寺里的穆斯林共庆每年一度的纳乌鲁斯节（突厥民族的传统节日）时，协助清真寺的伊玛目（即教长）举行了穆斯林特有的敬拜仪式，<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，遂被伊犁州巩留县吉尔格郎乡警方抓走，同期该村清真寺里的教长及<span lang="EN-US">4</span>名穆斯林亦被抓走，并被悉数送进当地一所“再教育营”接受洗脑培训和关押，自此失联；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年获悉，其等一行<span lang="EN-US">6</span>人已被伊犁州巩留县警方以涉嫌“非法集会，传扬不正当的宗教等”罪名拘捕，后被伊犁州巩留县检察院起诉至巩留县法院；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">-3</span>月，其等<span lang="EN-US">6</span>人被伊犁州巩留县法院以“非法集会罪”和“非法传播宗教罪”分别密判<span lang="EN-US">18</span>年<span lang="EN-US">-21</span>年不等刑期，其中，木拉提别克•吾麻尔被重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">18</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2036</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月；据悉，自其被抓判后，其妻子和两个孩子的生活陷入困境，其妹亦因受牵连而被迫在亲戚邻里家辗转借宿。目前在新疆新源监狱（新疆伊犁新源县喀拉布拉镇，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">835813</span>）服刑。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/09/18.html"><b><span color="windowtext" face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/09/18.html</span></b></a></span><b><u><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">穆萨江·伊玛目（维吾尔）：</span></b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">新疆维吾尔自治区乌鲁木齐市人，维吾尔族名<span lang="EN-US"> Musajan Imam</span>，伊哈拉斯<span lang="EN-US">Ihlas</span>便利连锁店创始人与法人代表，维吾尔商人，著名慈善企业家，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年初，曾因与在土耳其经商的兄弟合作，在新疆乌鲁木齐市建造用于商贸活动的建筑大楼，并将土耳其乌力克尔<span lang="EN-US"> Ulker</span>食品饮料公司生产的品牌食品推向新疆维吾尔自治区市场，故而备受当时新疆当局的称许，并被誉为“改革开放的典范”；<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年，其投资创立伊哈拉斯专业发展公司<span lang="EN-US">Ihlas ProfessionalDevelopment Company</span>，因与土耳其乌力克尔<span lang="EN-US">lker</span>等公司合作，随很快使其公司发展为在新疆多地（如乌鲁木齐、喀什、和田、吐鲁番、哈密等城市）拥有共计<span lang="EN-US">50 </span>个批发市场、<span lang="EN-US">500</span>多家食品店和<span lang="EN-US">200</span>条产品线的知名便利连锁公司；又因其公司<span lang="EN-US">1</span>直是当地经济的龙头企业，能为新疆的许多年轻维吾尔人创造丰富的就业机会，并为解决交通等问题而在阿克苏地区的阿图什市阿扎克乡铺设道路、修建水塔，还对许多贫困维吾尔大学生提供大笔求学经费，对喀什、和田及阿图什市的贫困人口等提供每年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>亿多元人民币的救助资金，故而成为有很高知名度和影响力的慈善企业家；然而，自<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年新疆政治气氛开始紧张和中共当局调派新的管理者以加强对新疆各少数民族的管控以来，其言行成为当局眼中需要打击的“可疑对象”；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，被乌鲁木齐市警方从伊哈拉斯公司办公室带走刑拘；后被乌鲁木齐市检察院正式批捕，被指控因其与土耳其方面的商业贸易往来及相关人员有“可疑关系”，主指与其有业务往来的土耳其方人员的信息及对话，尤其是与曾在<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年—<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年期间负责对外贸易的土耳其前国务部长库尔萨德•图兹曼的对话内容等，显示有触犯相关法律的嫌疑；另有其他“问题”，比如其在新疆故意扩大清真食品方面的作用，其个人装饰建筑物的维吾尔风格及所属企业、民族身份认同等与政府所要求的观念不合，以及对捐资给不同组织的天课（天课指伊斯兰教义里要求凡达到特定数额财产的人，就要拿出特定数额的财产，无偿给予特定的人群）不认同，等等，亦成为其罪状之<span lang="EN-US">1</span>；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，被乌鲁木齐市中级法院<span lang="EN-US">1</span>审以“与土耳其有可疑关系” 罪名等秘密重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">17</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2035</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日；另悉，其儿子、侄子、女婿等亦与其<span lang="EN-US">1</span>同被抓捕、判刑。目前服刑监狱缺详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/12/176.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span color="windowtext" face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/12/176.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> <o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 22pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">N.<o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">纳杂尔•叶尔江（哈萨克）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">那艳</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">乃比江•艾比布拉（维）</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 267.5pt;"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">南杰顿珠（藏）、</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">南民民</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<span lang="EN-US"><span style="mso-tab-count: 1;">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">聂丽娜、</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">聂梅凤、</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">宁惠荣、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">牛腾宇、</span><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">努尔哈因﹒木哈麦提沙尔（哈萨克）、</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">努尔莫哈提•亚辛</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">努尔兰（哈萨克）、</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">诺布•顿珠（藏）</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">纳杂尔﹒叶尔江：</span></b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">他与哈纳提别克﹒萨布尔别克、阿尔恒﹒巴杂尔别克、乌木别提﹒卡斯木、哈伊拉提别克﹒木合塔尔汗、沙部旦﹒沙伊合、耶尔肯别克﹒达列力、肯杰别克﹒达列力、玛乌提﹒么斯尔汗都是新疆伊利市哈萨克自治州阿尔泰市巴里巴盖乡人，哈萨克族，穆斯林。其中，纳杂尔﹒叶尔江<span lang="EN-US">26</span>岁，哈纳提别克﹒萨布尔别克<span lang="EN-US">26</span>岁，阿尔恒﹒巴杂尔别克<span lang="EN-US">27</span>岁，乌木别提﹒卡斯木<span lang="EN-US">31</span>岁，哈伊拉提别克﹒木合塔尔汗<span lang="EN-US">37</span>岁，沙部旦﹒沙伊合约<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁，耶尔肯别克﹒达列力<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁，肯杰别克﹒达列力<span lang="EN-US">27</span>岁，玛乌提﹒么斯尔汗约<span lang="EN-US">30</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">-8</span>月，因他们分别在私下里进行了穆斯林传统常规祷告仪式，而被中共新疆伊犁市哈萨克自治州阿尔泰当局知晓后拘捕，遂很快被阿尔泰市地方法院以“非法从事宗教活动”和“从事宗教极端活动”为由分别判处<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">-6</span>年不等刑期。目前各人具体判刑不详，刑至日期不详，服刑监狱不详，服刑状况及健康程度等不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">那艳：</span></b><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">2022</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年四十多岁，是沈阳市第六医院的护士。王荣军、那艳母女俩于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日左右失踪。亲朋好友到处寻找，从那艳工作单位，到派出所，到街道，没有任何人提供讯息。直到<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，亲属才得到母女俩被绑架并被判刑的确切消息。现在她们仍被非法关押在沈阳市第一看守所。王荣军及女儿那艳已分别被辽中区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月。刑期到：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/5/22/443930.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span color="windowtext" face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/5/22/443930.html</span></b></a></span><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">乃比江•艾比布拉：</span></b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">维族，<span lang="EN-US">1983</span>年出生，新疆和田地区洛浦县人，前新疆师范大学、新疆大学和中央民族大学老师，新疆大学优秀本科生导师和研究员，维吾尔语言学教授，中国在押政治犯。早年，曾就读于新疆维吾尔自治区和田师范技术高中中文专业，并于<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年毕业；<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">-2014</span>年，曾出国留学在德国哥廷根大学攻读博士学位；毕业后又返回新疆；据悉，回国前，曾有多个友人警告他说，“新疆局势正在恶化，建议还是留在德国而不是回国找工作”；但其对此则认为，“若只专注于学术研究，远离社会冲突和其他当局认为有争议的问题，回国仍是安全的”；基于其认为自己回国可以做得更好，且相信通过对维吾尔学生的教授，可以为他们提供更上一层楼的社会机会及工作舞台，<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年，随毅然返回新疆；回国后，曾先后在新疆师范大学、新疆大学和中央民族大学学习与工作；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，曾因完成一篇题为《汉译佛经中古维吾尔语动词的词典意义》的博士论文，从而获取了<span lang="EN-US">4</span>项研究资助，并在著名学术期刊上发表了<span lang="EN-US">10</span>多篇文章；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月，因中共当局对新疆维吾尔族、哈萨克斯坦族、回族等各族群开始大规模实行“再教育营”（中共称之为“职业技能教育培训机构”）的集中高压管控政策，遂与多位大学其他主要教师及研究人员悉数被警方传唤到所在大学保卫处，并在短暂审讯后被乌鲁木齐市国家安全局警员带走，后送“再教育营”进行洗脑式培训，自此失联；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，知其被新疆乌鲁木齐市法院秘密重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年，罪名不清，服刑截止日期不清；亲友疑其被拘捕判刑与在德国学习期间，其接触了突厥学家阿不都外力，并对维吾尔文化做了大量研究所致。目前服刑监狱不明。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/15.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span color="windowtext" face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/09/15.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">南杰顿珠（藏）：</span></b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">出生年月不详，四川省甘孜藏族自治州炉霍县人，炉霍寺僧人，中国在押良心犯。由于中共当局在西藏及其周边各省涉藏地区强硬推行“爱国和法制宣传教育”活动，引发多地藏民强烈不满，四川省甘孜州炉霍县藏民于<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日（即当年中国农历新年初一）举行大规模和平示威活动；该活动立即惨遭当地警方严厉的武力镇压和任意抓捕，致使上百藏人被抓，多人被打死打伤；至同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，共有<span lang="EN-US">36</span>人被中共当局判处<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>个月直至无期徒刑不等的刑期，另有数人被捕后完全失踪；南杰顿珠亦因积极参与抗议示威游行，于<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月被警方以“参与和带头示威活动”为由从当地炉霍寺抓走刑拘；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，被甘孜藏族自治州炉霍县法院以“炉火示威活动的主要带头人”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年。目前在四川省甘孜藏族自治州康定县监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">南民民：</span></b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 106%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，<b>广东</b></span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">深圳法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1957</span>年生，退休会计，原住址湖北省罗田县凤上镇白龙井巷<span lang="EN-US">19</span>号。南民民<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年开始修炼法轮功后，<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年中共迫害法轮功后，她曾被判刑两次，共<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年。南民民于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日被警察抓捕，被关押至罗湖看守所，后转到深圳市第<span lang="EN-US">3</span>看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，她被转至盐田看守所。后一审被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。南民民被判刑后上诉，二审法庭于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月宣布维持原判。南民民于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月份被转至广州女子监狱继续迫害。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源</b>：</span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/6/%E6%9B%BE%E9%81%AD%E5%8D%81%E5%B9%B4%E5%86%A4%E5%88%91-%E6%B7%B1%E5%9C%B3%E9%80%80%E4%BC%91%E4%BC%9A%E8%AE%A1%E5%8D%97%E6%B0%91%E6%B0%91%E5%8F%88%E8%A2%AB%E8%AF%AC%E5%88%A4%E4%BA%94%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-440974.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span color="windowtext" face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/6/%E6%9B%BE%E9%81%AD%E5%8D%81%E5%B9%B4%E5%86%A4%E5%88%91-%E6%B7%B1%E5%9C%B3%E9%80%80%E4%BC%91%E4%BC%9A%E8%AE%A1%E5%8D%97%E6%B0%91%E6%B0%91%E5%8F%88%E8%A2%AB%E8%AF%AC%E5%88%A4%E4%BA%94%E5%B9%B4%E5%8D%8A-440974.html</span></b></a></span><b mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">聂丽娜：</span></b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河南访民。聂丽娜在<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年开始举报村委支书师海法、村主任郭安祥等倒卖土地，侵害其宅基地的不法行为，期间遭到无数次的打击报复，及判刑迫害，其多位家人也同样遭到地方政府株连九族方式的打击报复，及黑社会的暴力伤害。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日上午<span lang="EN-US">8</span>点，聂丽娜到国家信访局和中纪委信访举报，遭到北京警察<span lang="EN-US">(</span>警号<span lang="EN-US">023359)</span>阻拦，聂丽娜就拨打<span lang="EN-US">12345</span>市长热线和北京警务督察电话，被强制带走后交给举报人带回许昌市襄城县关押黑监狱，十五天后转刑事拘留至今。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日上午九点，已关押<span lang="EN-US">15</span>个月的聂丽娜涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”案，在许昌市鄢陵县法院<span lang="EN-US">3</span>号审判庭开庭。未宣判。</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">后于<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日上午在许昌市看守所被鄢陵县法院秘密宣判——聂丽娜被以寻衅滋事罪判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日。<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日当天法院直接将判决书送到许昌市看守所，通过看守所交给聂丽娜，但聂丽娜拒绝签字。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/04/4.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span color="windowtext" face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/04/4.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">聂梅凤：</span></b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">河北石家庄市正定县善良法轮功学员，女。<span lang="EN-US">1963</span>年生，是正定县文物旅游局文保所开元寺职工，现已退休。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，张彦芹、聂梅凤在恒丰翠庭小区发放法轮功真相资料时，被抓捕到正定县公安分局。随后，张彦芹、聂梅凤被抄家。<span lang="EN-US"> 2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，张彦芹、聂梅凤被开庭，判聂梅凤<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，从<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日起；判张彦芹<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，从<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日起，说是张彦芹有过前科所以判的重些。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/12/18/453251.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span color="windowtext" face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/12/18/453251.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">宁惠荣：</span></b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">男，满族人，基督徒，出生于<span lang="EN-US">1946</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，原籍北京市，<span lang="EN-US">1966</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月赴新疆“支边”，供职于新疆哈密地区盐化工厂。<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年，因抗议警察滥权的行为，走上维权之路。<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年开始赴北京投诉。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，向北京市治安总队提交“游行示威”的申请报告，被指控“寻衅滋事”，遭到逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月，被新疆地方当局判处三年半监禁，在新疆吐鲁番监狱服刑，因拒不认罪，未获减刑，<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月刑满出狱。宁惠荣于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日在永定门长途汽车站，被劫访人员从<span lang="EN-US">102</span>路电车上劫走，<span lang="EN-US">&nbsp;9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日被强行带回哈密后，被关押在哈密市公安局派出所，平板电脑、手机、钱包被扣押。宁惠荣因对哈密法院的枉法判决，在向最高人民法院申诉。他们就先抓人，再找罪名，关押至<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日下午，宁惠荣被送到哈密市医院，以治病的名义继续关押，白天二个人看守夜间三个人看守，人身自由被非法限制，至今仍被非法拘禁。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">牛腾宇</span></b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日出生，山西省晋城市高平市人，有“计算机天才”之称，恶俗维基服务器运维技术人员，“恶俗维基”站长，“恶俗维基网站恶势力犯罪集团案”主要受害人，在押中国政治犯。自<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年起，中国大陆及海外有网友开始频繁尝试搭建和运作被称为“恶俗圈”的网络平台，其中“恶俗维基”、“支那维基”和“红岸基金会”三大网站最为知名；此期间，因其对计算机技术的痴迷与天赋，以及网站宗旨是“揭露并记录事实”，随加入“恶俗维基”网站，并成为该网站技术维护员及站长；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年，曾因多家“恶俗圈”网站频发习近平及家人、和中共高官及家属的户籍和照片等信息，其所在“恶俗维基”网站亦将此类信息挂于网上，遂引发中共当局的极端不满与监控；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，又因其在香港爆发“反送中”大游行之后，与“恶俗维基”创办人肖彦锐相约前去香港，对香港大游行进行围观了解，返回后虽又于同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月初至<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日到日本一游，但回国一周后；<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，其网站全部会员尽被各地警方突然抓捕，其亦被广东省茂名市警方抓捕，并遭毒打；同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，被以涉嫌“帮助信息网络犯罪活动罪”刑拘，关押于茂名市第一看守所；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，被茂名市检察院以同罪名予以批捕，指控其曾在恶俗维基网上“共发表评论<span lang="EN-US">8</span>条，上传图片<span lang="EN-US">20</span>张，共有<span lang="EN-US">748</span>条的用户贡献，其本人有<span lang="EN-US">285</span>条贡献值”等讯息，散布虚假信息，恶毒攻击、诋毁政府和国家领导人及其家属形象等，是“恶俗维基网站恶势力犯罪集团案”主犯，故而应予逮捕和判刑；同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，经茂名市检察院批准被延长侦查羁押期限<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个月；<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，又被广东省佛山市警方以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”被指定监视居住，并转关至佛山市南海区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，其被解除被指定监视居住，同日又被茂名市警方再次逮捕；同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，其一行<span lang="EN-US">24</span>人“涉恶势力犯罪集团案”在广东省茂名市法院开庭受审，至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，其案<span lang="EN-US">24</span>人均被宣判，其中，其被以“寻衅滋事罪”（判<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年）、“侵犯个人信息罪”（判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年）、“非法经营罪”（判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年），最终决定执行有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年，并处罚金人民币<span lang="EN-US">13</span>万；其等均表不服，立刻上诉；据悉，其被重判与曾发布中共高层个人信息、镇压香港及新疆等内容有关，且二审法院拟对其速审速决，极有可能维持原判，后二审果然维持原判；另据悉，<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日到<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日期间，为令其屈打成招，曾遭长期刑讯逼供，被吊打致残；刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2033</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。先被羁押于茂名市第一看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月后被送到了广东省肇庆市四会监狱。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">努尔哈因﹒木哈麦提沙尔（哈萨克）：</span></b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">新疆伊利市哈萨克自治州阿尔泰市人，<span lang="EN-US">60</span>岁左右，哈萨克族，穆斯林。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">-8</span>月，中共新疆伊犁哈萨克自治州当局判处了一批穆斯林仪式祷告者，指控其因非法从事了穆斯林式常规祷告仪式，涉嫌法宗教活动或极端宗教活动。其中，努尔哈因﹒木哈麦提沙尔因在家里存有《古兰经》，被警方搜出，随被抓捕，现已被哈萨克自治州法院以“从事极端宗教活动”等为由秘密判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">努尔莫哈提•亚辛：</span></b><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1974</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日出生，新疆维吾尔自治区喀什地区巴楚县人，又名努尔莫哈迈提•雅辛、努力默赫默德•亚森，维吾尔族名<span lang="EN-US">Nurmuhemmet Yasin</span>，笔名欧尔开西，维吾尔族知名自由作家、诗人、散文家和记者，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2004</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年，曾因在《喀什噶尔文学》杂志上发表一篇寓言体小说《野鸽子》（<span lang="EN-US">Yawa Kepter</span>），随被中共新疆当局认为其内容批评了新疆地方政府的管理现状，<span lang="EN-US">2004</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，被喀什地区巴楚县警方以涉嫌“煽动分裂主义罪”抓捕、刑拘；后被喀什地区检察院以同罪名转正式批捕，指控其因小说内容有主张维吾尔族独立的思想意味，故而其言行属于违法；<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2 </span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，被新疆喀什地区中级法院以“煽动分裂国家罪”、“煽动民族仇恨、民族歧视罪”秘密判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年；其不服上诉；喀什地区中级法院原打算对其减刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，但因遭时任中共喀什地区党委书记的强烈反对，随二审依然维持原判；据悉，其聘请代理律师权被剥夺，狱中惨遭殴打；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月，曾有消息误传其死于狱中，但其一亲属则表示，<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月家人曾去探监，见其身体状况似乎良好，且同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，又收到一封来自狱中的家信，认为此信应是他本人所写；原本应于<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日刑满释放，但截至<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，其仍在狱中服刑，仅因狱中很难被允许探视且新疆对外信息难以联络，故其因何一直不被释放以及后续情况缺详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">目前在新疆乌鲁木齐市第一监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/04/10_24.html"><b><span color="windowtext" face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/04/10_24.html</span></b></a></span><u><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">努尔兰：</span></b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">全名是哈德力别克·努尔兰。<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年代出生，新疆维吾尔自治区阿尔泰地区青河县查干郭勒乡人，哈萨克族，穆斯林，乌鲁木齐市酷巴巴网络科技有限公司创办人，企业家，中国在押良心犯。早期曾就读于东北大学，<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年毕业；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年，曾前往新疆乌鲁木齐市创业，后创办酷巴巴网络科技有限公司；<span lang="EN-US"> 2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，曾因宗教信仰而做礼拜（即穆斯林进行敬拜时的祷告方式），被阿尔泰地区青河县当局很快知晓，随被青河县警方带走拘留，并被送进“再教育营”进行洗脑式教育，自此失联；因其在“再教育营”拒绝接受洗脑教育，遂被警方以“从事非法宗教活动”为罪由转为正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月，被新疆维吾尔自治区阿尔泰地区青河县法院重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月；据悉，其被判刑前后，家属均未收到任何法律文书，家属欲为其聘请辩护律师遭拒，探视权被剥夺，至今不让会面。目前在新疆克拉玛依市监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">诺布•顿珠：</span></b><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1956</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，藏族名<span lang="EN-US">NorbuDondrup</span>，西藏日喀则市定日县人，日喀则市定日县协格尔镇查那村当卓寺（藏民称之为登卓寺（<span lang="EN-US">Tengdro</span>））寺院法师，公益慈善捐助人，藏族异见人士，中国在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">-9</span>月，曾因当卓寺僧侣曲嘉旺波（<span lang="EN-US">Choegyal Wangpo</span>）到西藏首府拉萨市做佛事访问时不甚将手机遗失在某咖啡馆，后被老板交予拉萨市警方处置；但因警方在查阅其手机时，发现手机里存有其及当卓寺僧侣与尼泊尔同乡藏僧有过密联系的信息记录，尤其是存有<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月尼泊尔大地震时，他们向那里的藏民和寺院捐款赈灾等记录，以及还存有和第<span lang="EN-US">14</span>世达赖喇嘛有关的图片及文献等，遂立即触碰到中共西藏当局的政治敏感神经，认定这是一起与境外敌对势力勾结，利用网络通讯对国家安全构成威胁的典型案件；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，诺布•顿珠所在寺庙突然遭到日喀则市当局派出的多名武警及公安警察袭击，所有僧人均被强迫接受政治洗脑教育数天，多人遭殴打，且其被殴打成重伤；之后有<span lang="EN-US">20</span>名僧侣（含其在内）被刑拘，当卓寺及其附近的网络被切断；三天后，除一名僧侣因向当局抗议而自杀，其余<span lang="EN-US">19</span>名僧人仍被超押，数月不放；后其与曲嘉旺波等<span lang="EN-US">4</span>名藏僧均被日喀则市检察院以涉嫌“跟境外藏人联系、赈济尼泊尔地震，或拥有和达赖喇嘛有关照片或文献”为罪由正式批捕，自此失联<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日获悉，其等<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人案统一在日喀则中级法院开庭审理，最终被以“危害国家安全罪” 重判<span lang="EN-US">20</span>年<span lang="EN-US">-5</span>年不等刑期，其中，诺布•顿珠被判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">17</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2036</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月。目前疑似在拉萨市札基监狱服刑。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/06/17.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span color="windowtext" face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/06/17.html</span></b></a></span><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 22pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">O</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 22pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">．<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">欧彪峰、</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">欧道齐、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">欧彪峰：</span></b><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1980</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日出生，湖南省株洲市人，人称“小彪”，湖南省宁乡市黑金时代小区居民，人权捍卫者，“公民运动”践行者，中国在押政治犯。近年来，曾因积极参与公民维权活动，经常发布被中共当局打压的公民行动者的第一手信息，随遭湖南省当局的维稳监控；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月及<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，曾因为公开声援许志永和常玮平等良心犯而被当地警方传唤；同年，曾因声援香港反送中运动，并在香港著名媒体大亨、社会活动家黎智英被抓捕后，公开表态支持黎智英及香港《苹果日报》，而遭湖南警方多次警告，并被威胁、暗示当局正在搜寻对其实施抓捕的证据；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，因关注并协助曾于<span lang="EN-US">2018 </span>年在上海街头向习近平肖像泼墨而被“维稳”（即被当局非法关进精神病医院）的“泼墨女孩”董瑶琼，在推特上发求救呼吁，随立遭当局的严厉打压，被湖南省株洲市芦淞区警方从在宁乡市的家中带走传唤；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，被以“寻衅滋事”罪由处行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天，其家被查抄；同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，又被株洲市芦淞区警方以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”转为指定居所监视居住；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被芦淞区警方以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”转为刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，又被株洲市芦淞区检察院以同罪名予以批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，其案在湖南省株洲市监管中心内宣判，欧彪峰获刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。目前被羁押于株洲市公安局监管中心看守所。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/12/36.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span color="windowtext" face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/12/36.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">欧道齐：</span></b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">湖南省怀化市沅陵县官庄镇人，现居长沙开办少儿培训中心。年约<span lang="EN-US">40</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>、<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日间被警方带走，罪名为“寻衅滋事”。欧道齐在长沙的培训机构与铺面也被查封。知情人说，<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，欧道齐所在的怀化地区老乡群中一网名为“糟老头子”的网友在聊天过程中以一句“习近平上台搞什么都犯法”，来表达对现实社会风声鹤唳草木皆兵的统治手法不满，其后该名友遭到警方抓捕，并有知情群员将警方的核查通报上传至该群组。随后多名网友将该图片转发到其他社交平台，其中就包括欧道齐。据称欧道齐将图片上传发布在推特后不久便被警方发现，并根据<span lang="EN-US">IP</span>地址将其拘捕。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 22pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">P</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">．<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">潘冬梅、</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">潘惠玲</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">潘晶</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">、<span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">潘西华</span></span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">潘玉峰、潘自争、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; minor-fareast;">彭桦英、彭敬军</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">、</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">彭乐宽、</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">彭立发</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">、</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">彭石清、</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">普化（藏）、<span mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">卜永柱</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormalCxSpMiddle" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8pt; mso-add-space: auto; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">潘冬梅：</span></b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">广东省茂名市袂花镇法轮功学员。一九八零年出生，家住茂名市茂南区袂花镇坡仔村，在袂花镇市场经营蔬菜摊位谋生。她有四个小孩，是个勤劳的母亲，贤惠的妻子，孝顺的儿媳。潘冬梅自中共迫害法轮功以来，因为坚持修炼法轮功，遭多次骚扰和迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日被茂名市公安局高新区分局、七迳派出所警察抓捕，关押到茂名市第一看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，她被茂南区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年、罚金一万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormalCxSpMiddle" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8pt; mso-add-space: auto; mso-pagination: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">潘惠玲：</span></b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">广州市荔湾区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1947</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月中共当局镇压法轮功。其遭多次迫害，曾被劳教<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，潘惠玲出去宣讲法轮功，遭白云区警察抓捕，曾经被关押在广州市第一看守所，后获悉被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/4/12/458723.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormalCxSpMiddle" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8pt; mso-add-space: auto; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: 0pt;">辽宁省丹东市法轮功学员<b>。</b><span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日被抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">潘西华：</span></b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黑龙江鸡西市法轮功学员陈维权、潘西华夫妇，于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日遭滴道区国保金辉等警察抓捕抢劫、关押构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日被密山市法院开庭，判陈维权<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年、潘西华<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/25/%E9%BB%91%E9%BE%99%E6%B1%9F%E9%B8%A1%E8%A5%BF%E5%B8%82%E9%99%88%E7%BB%B4%E6%9D%83%E3%80%81%E6%BD%98%E8%A5%BF%E5%8D%8E%E5%A4%AB%E5%A6%87%E8%A2%AB%E8%AF%AC%E5%88%A4%E4%B8%83%E5%B9%B4%E3%80%81%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4-441692.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span color="windowtext" face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/25/%E9%BB%91%E9%BE%99%E6%B1%9F%E9%B8%A1%E8%A5%BF%E5%B8%82%E9%99%88%E7%BB%B4%E6%9D%83%E3%80%81%E6%BD%98%E8%A5%BF%E5%8D%8E%E5%A4%AB%E5%A6%87%E8%A2%AB%E8%AF%AC%E5%88%A4%E4%B8%83%E5%B9%B4%E3%80%81%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4-441692.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">潘玉峰：</span></b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁朝阳市两法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日下午，潘玉峰在家中被北塔分局警察抓捕。潘玉峰是位难得的孝子，家中老母亲患老年痴呆，生活不能自理，一直由潘玉峰照顾。自潘玉峰被绑架后，老人无人照顾，很快消瘦了很多，在潘玉峰绑架近一年后老人悲苦离开人世，临终都未见到儿子一面。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，潘玉峰案开庭，律师做无罪辩护。后得知潘玉峰被双塔法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">潘自争：</span></b><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1952</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日出生，江西省上饶市广信区清水乡常阜村人，南昌市西湖区星河国际<span lang="EN-US">B</span>座<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>室居民，基督徒，江西省南昌市基督教召会负责人和教会长老，“南昌召会教案”当事人，中国在押良心犯。很早即笃信基督教，并在当地教会积极参与侍奉活动；后离开家乡到江西省南昌市生活，并成为南昌基督教召会（又名“呼喊派”、“神的教会”、“地方召会”）骨干信徒；<span lang="EN-US">1995</span>年起，因中共当局将“地方召会”确定为邪教组织“呼喊派”，遂其等所在江西众召会同工及信徒均遭逼迫，迫使教会只能转为地下教会，同时设立上饶召会、南昌召会和九江召会等多个召会；在此期间，其被按立为教会长老；自<span lang="EN-US">2011</span>年始，其被选任为“呼喊派”南昌召会负责人，因其努力扩展教会规模，故而很快发展出昌北区、红谷滩区、湾里区、文教路区等<span lang="EN-US"> 9</span>个区召会；然而因其所在南昌召会规模不断扩大，其等教会领袖、同工及众信徒频遭当地政府监控、打压；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，其所在召会的几个聚会点突遭南昌市经济技术开发区警方查抄，当场搜走《生命读经》、《圣经恢复本》等<span lang="EN-US">204</span>本呼喊派教会书籍及宣传品；后其与聚会点信徒黄华二人被带走传唤；同年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，其二人均被南昌市经济技术开发区警方以涉嫌“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天；后黄华获取保候审，但其仍被续押至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日；后其二人又被警方反复收押、保释；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年，其案被当地警方移送到检察院审查，但证据不足，同年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，其二人再被南昌市西湖区检察院继续取保候审；<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年初，其二人被正式收监逮捕，当局被指控因其等带领聚会时人数超过百人，与中共当局的宗教规定相抵触，故应予以逮捕法办；<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，其案一审在南昌市西湖区法院开庭审理，至<span lang="EN-US"> 5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，其二人均被宣判，其中，其被以“组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">30000</span>元，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日；黄华亦被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">25000</span>元。目前疑似被羁押于南昌市第一看守所。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/07/36.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span color="windowtext" face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/07/36.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">庞健：</span></b><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1991</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，河北省保定市人，保定市高碑店市泗庄镇庞场村居民，天主教徒，教名“雅各布布布伯（<span lang="EN-US">Jacob</span>）”，网名“雅格比约”，笔名“高阳”， “幽燕民族主义”（<span lang="EN-US">Yuyencianism</span>）认同者，“幽燕独立运动”<span lang="EN-US">(Yuyencia Independence Movement)</span>倡导者，中国社会问题关切者，农村强拆问题独立调查员，自由撰稿人，中国在押政治犯。多年来，一直热衷于中国社会问题的关注和调研，并持有本土主义理念，主张“幽燕独立”（即一种支持“幽燕民族独立”<span lang="EN-US"> (Yuyencia Independence Movement)</span>的政治主张）；曾以笔名“高阳”发表过不少与京津冀之地文史、民俗和宗教相关的作品；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月，曾以教名“雅各布布布伯（<span lang="EN-US">Jacob</span>）”接受香港电台《铿锵集》栏目采访，介绍河北天主教地下教会的情况；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，又以笔名“高阳”接受自由亚洲电台采访，讲述自己通过三年多独立调查了解到的京津冀一带农村遭强拆的情况；因其频繁接受外电专访，并在国际上产生了一定影响，随立遭中共河北当局的强烈打压；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，被当地高碑店市警方以涉嫌“煽动分裂国家罪”刑拘，自此失联；同年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，又被高碑店市检察院更换罪名，以涉嫌“分裂国家罪”予以正式批捕；超押至今，一直不予释放，亦无其更多被押具体信息。目前被羁押于河北省高碑店市看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/06/blog-post_29.html"><b><span color="windowtext" face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/06/blog-post_29.html</span></b></a></span><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b><span color="windowtext" face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">庞友：</span></b><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1963</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，又名庞有，陕西省延安市宜川县籍人，北京市昌平区宏福苑小区公民，原北京市朝阳区洼里乡政府（现奥运村街道办事处）规划办公室主任，后任北京市旭日房地产有限责任公司经理，法轮功信仰者，原北京市朝阳区北苑大羊坊法轮功炼功点义务辅导员，中国在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年代，因锻炼和追求信仰法轮功而屡遭当局拘捕和酷刑打压并被撤销公职；<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月至<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，曾被北京市朝阳区警方<span lang="EN-US">4</span>次非法拘押，并在抄家时将其私有贵重财产侵吞占有，至今无一说法；关押期间，曾被多次毒打，并惨遭电棍电击全身等酷刑；<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，曾因在天安门广场拉横幅为法轮功正名而和平请愿吁呼，故而连续遭广场便衣警察及通州某派出所警方暴力殴打致昏迷；后被关押于通州乔庄看守所期间，为胁迫其放弃法轮功信仰，又连续遭警方恶意暴打、电棍电击及强行灌食等非人道逼迫；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，曾因在家制作法轮功信仰者遭迫害讯息，而再遭北京市朝阳区警方抓捕，并被施以酷刑，最终导致其一只胳膊残废不能动，之后被北京市高级法院以“邪教罪”枉法重判<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，后送北京市前进监狱服刑；刑满出狱后，<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，又因自由信仰事宜而被北京市朝阳区警方拘捕，后被朝阳区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年；第二次出狱后，<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，因其曾陪同亲戚在陕西老家拜访生意上的朋友，并讲述法轮功遭逼迫的事实真相，遂被延安市宜川县警方传唤带走，后被刑拘于陕西省黄龙县看守所和宜川县看守所共计<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并再遭多种酷刑虐折磨，令其痛不欲生；之后其案被地方检察院起诉和移交至陕西省黄龙县法院，最终经次年北京<span lang="EN-US">1004</span>名普通民众的紧急呼吁签名和著名人权律师对其案的有力辩护与质询，<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，宜川县法院对其案下达了无罪释放判决书；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月、<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，因参加法轮功家庭式交流聚会和向他人宣传法轮功信息，而曾两次又被当地警方刑拘，后获释；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，再度被北京市昌平区警方以涉嫌邪教罪拘捕；现其案已被当地检察院提起公诉，且被移交至京市昌平区法院，至今未审待判；据悉，数年来其曾无数次遭绑架和非法关押，并曾被两次枉法冤判共计<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年，其家人因其被判备受威胁，以致于其母亲因多次受惊吓而含恨离世，其妻子也被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，其幼小儿子因父母均被抓走判刑，仅留下他一人在家，故至今仍有心理疾患。目前庞友被羁押于北京市昌平区看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/01/12.html"><b><span color="windowtext" face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/01/12.html</span></b></a></span><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b><span color="windowtext" face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast; text-decoration: none; text-underline: none;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">彭彪：</span></b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">贵州省六盘水市盘州市城关镇法轮功学员。彭彪于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，被盘州市公安局绑架，而后被送至六盘水市第二看守所关押、构陷迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日左右，由六盘水市第二看守所通知，彭彪被六盘水市中级法院判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。现彭彪被非法关押在贵州省都匀监狱六监区迫害。据悉彭彪现被<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个刑事犯包夹迫害。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">彭桦英：</span></b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">四川省巴中市法轮功学员，女，巴中市统计局公务员（主任科员）。彭桦英女士，在街上给人讲法轮功真相时，被不明真相的人恶意举报，于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日遭抓捕，后彭桦英被秘密判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/10/2/450322.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span color="windowtext" face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/10/2/450322.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">彭敬军：</span></b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河北深泽县彭赵庄村法轮功学员。彭敬军<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日被抓捕，一直被关押在深泽县看守所，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月十四日在晋州市法院被开庭，律师为他做了无罪辩护。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月得知，彭敬军被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/6/5/461627.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span color="windowtext" face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/6/5/461627.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">彭乐宽：</span></b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">山东招远市城区法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1954</span>年生，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年六十八岁。在中共对法轮功持续至今二十多年的迫害中，彭乐宽曾两次被判五年，遭<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年冤狱迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日（正月十五日）中午，在自己的家中被招远市泉山派出所的多个警察抓捕，后得知彭乐宽被栖霞法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/26/%E6%9B%BE%E4%BA%8C%E6%AC%A1%E8%A2%AB%E5%88%A4%E4%BA%94%E5%B9%B4-%E5%B1%B1%E4%B8%9C%E6%8B%9B%E8%BF%9C%E5%B8%82%E5%BD%AD%E4%B9%90%E5%AE%BD%E5%8F%88%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4-440504.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span color="windowtext" face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/3/26/%E6%9B%BE%E4%BA%8C%E6%AC%A1%E8%A2%AB%E5%88%A4%E4%BA%94%E5%B9%B4-%E5%B1%B1%E4%B8%9C%E6%8B%9B%E8%BF%9C%E5%B8%82%E5%BD%AD%E4%B9%90%E5%AE%BD%E5%8F%88%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4-440504.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">彭立发</span></b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：网名彭载舟，<span lang="EN-US">1974</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日出生，黑龙江省泰来县宁姜蒙古族乡勤俭村<span lang="EN-US">737</span>组人，北京市西城区长住居民，北京甜瓜网络技术有限公司员工，北京四通桥倒习勇士，民主人权斗士，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，中共“二十大”即将召开之际，因其在北京市中关村四通桥上勇敢挂两条红字横幅，一条写着“不要核酸要吃饭！不要封锁要自由！不要谎言要尊严！不要文革要改革！不要领袖要选票！不做奴才做公民！”，另一条写着“罢课罢工罢免独裁国贼习近平”，并放烟火引人注意，遂引路人纷纷驻足、停车用手机拍录；后经路人将拍录视频及照片发于社交平台，立引网民疯转，当天即震惊世人，继而在国际各大媒体上广为报导；据此，因其果敢挂横幅呼吁倒习，并在此之前，已有计划、有目的、有选择的给部分网站和知名异见人士发出其事先准备好的《致全国同胞书》，内容直指习近平以袁世凯和金正恩为导师，“做着不穿黄袍穿西装的皇帝梦”，呼吁全国军人和警察“像蔡锷、李烈钧、唐继尧一样勇敢，不要助纣为虐，不要为独裁者卖命，不要为独裁者当炮灰”，遂于当天很快被北京市西城区警方带走，自此失联；后此事件被海内外民众纷纷视为自<span lang="EN-US">1989</span>年六四事件以来，北京街头首次出现的直接挑战中共政权的横幅标语，并因是在中共二十大前保安级别明显升高戒备森严的时刻发生这一街头抗议事件，尤其令人震撼；截至当前，此事件影响仍在持续扩大，并在世界各地华人及留学生群体中掀起了纷纷效法倒习之势，但其本人被抓后的具体状况（比如涉嫌罪名、是否被刑讯逼供、身体是否酷刑及是否依然康健等等），音信全无。目前疑似被羁押于北京市西城区看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/11/blog-post_1.html"><b><span color="windowtext" face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/11/blog-post_1.html</span></b></a></span><b><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">彭石清：</span></b><a name="_Hlk512558029"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">湖南省湘潭市人，湘潭市岳塘区板塘花苑居民小区居民，某工厂木工，法轮功信仰者，良心犯。</span></a><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">因笃信法轮功而曾被当局多次抓捕关押，甚至曾被枉判<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，并先后在沅江赤山监狱、常德津市监狱服刑，备受酷刑虐待。出狱后，因其依然坚持信仰不变，遂遭当局更严厉监控打压。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日早，突然被湘潭市公安高新分局双马派出所警方数十人闯入家中，将其夫妇二人双双抓走，随后家被查抄，搜走相关法轮功资料数份，并将其所有存折、银行卡、社保卡、身份证等私人物品也一并搜走。当日其即被送往湘潭市看守所关押。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，其妻熊春霞在被索要了<span lang="EN-US">3000</span>元保释金后准予释放回家，而其竟被以涉邪教罪转正式批捕，被指控因制作和发放法轮功真相资料、印制有法轮功真相内容的人民币，以及发送法轮功真相内容短信等，因此违反了相关法律。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，其案在看守所内被湘潭市岳塘区法院秘密开庭，最终其被一审以“组织、利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年。目前被关押在湘潭市看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><a name="_Hlk122770476"><b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">彭树明：</span></b></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk122770476;"><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">1971</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk122770476;"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年出生，吉林省白城市洮南市籍人，长住山东省聊城市高唐县时风路团结小区，自办中医诊所医师，自由信仰追求者，法轮功信仰者，中国在押良心犯。早年自<span lang="EN-US">20</span>岁左右起，因师承一位老中医学习中医治疗，后在聊城市高唐县城开中医诊所行医<span lang="EN-US">20</span>余年，医治了许多疑难顽症患者，故而成为当地有口皆碑、受人尊敬和信任的好中医（大夫）；但自从<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年开始锻炼和信仰法轮功以来，屡遭山东当局关押和迫害；<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，曾因在当地高唐县城里喷法轮功宣传标语，而被高唐县人和派出所警方抓捕，并关押在高唐看守所，为此其曾绝食<span lang="EN-US">4</span>天反迫害；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，其在诊所行医时，又被高唐县汇鑫派出所警方莫名抓走，并被送高唐看守所关押；在被抓捕过程中，遂其在被非法关押在高唐看守所<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年多后，竟以此为因由被山东省高唐县法院，因一警察自己摔断脚脖子冤判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，后在当地聊城监狱服刑；刑满出狱后，其一边行医工作一边继续锻炼并宣传法轮功，故而遭到中共政府的<span lang="EN-US">610</span>法轮功监管办公室的更强烈的打压；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，因其用手机在微信中传播法轮功相关信息，被中共网警发现，遂被原籍吉林省洮南市警方跨省抓捕，后被以涉嫌“邪教罪”关押在吉林省白城市洮南市看守所；同年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，又被洮南市检察院以同罪名正式批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，其案被洮南市检察院提起公诉，并被移交至吉林省白城市洮南市法院；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，知其已被洮南市法院最终以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US"> 5</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日；据悉，其在洮南市看守所关押期间，曾屡遭犯人恶意毒打，警方却故意视而不见；其老母病故，妻子乳腺癌手术，家属多次请求让其回家探视一下，均遭拒绝；家属为其聘请律师作无罪辩护，亦被洮南市法院非法阻止。目前在山东省济南监狱服刑。</span></span><b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/12/5.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span color="windowtext" face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/12/5.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">彭宇华：</span></b><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1980</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日出生，湖北省籍人，理财经理，人权活动者。自<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年以来，因其创建了“两岸牵手”、“围观中国”、“围观华南”等系列<span lang="EN-US">QQ</span>群，并与李明哲等数十名境内外非政府组织成员及人权活动者，成立了旨在建立新型民主制度和进行中国大陆人权活动的“梅花公司”，遂被中共警方跟踪、监控。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日被湖南省长沙市国家安全局以涉嫌“颠覆国家政权罪”刑事拘留；同年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，被长沙市检察院以同罪名正式批捕，同日被长沙市警方正式逮捕，并指控其创建了系列<span lang="EN-US">QQ</span>群，炒作近年来大陆发生的热点事件，发布诋毁、攻击政府部门和大陆制度的言论，成立了“旨在颠覆大陆政权、推翻大陆基本政治制度的组织<span lang="EN-US">'</span>梅花公司<span lang="EN-US">'</span>”，制定了组织纲领，确定了组织框架和人员细致分工，组织<span lang="EN-US">100</span>万成员插手围观所谓热点事件，触犯了中国法律。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日其案在岳阳市中级法院开庭受审，同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日被该法院以“颠覆国家政权罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，剥权<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。对于一审他表示服从判决。目前被羁押于湖南省岳阳市看守所。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">普化（藏）：</span></b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">青海省黄南州同仁县多哇乡人，藏族人权捍卫者。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，中共<span lang="EN-US">18</span>大召开前夕、期间及之后，在藏区多地仅一个月内共发生了<span lang="EN-US">28</span>起自焚事件，当时同仁县就有<span lang="EN-US">9</span>位藏人自焚，其中多哇乡<span lang="EN-US">5</span>人自焚，均身亡。事发后，中共当局很快成立了青海省公安厅驻黄南州系列自焚案件专案组，并以涉嫌“散布自焚者照片并在照片上写下自焚者遗言”、“参与反政府示威抗议活动”等罪，抓捕藏民<span lang="EN-US">70</span>人。之后，有<span lang="EN-US">52</span>人被刑拘，有<span lang="EN-US">12</span>人被逮捕，普化即是其中宣布被正式逮捕者之一。<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，其多人在黄南州同仁县法院被宣判，普化被以不知名罪名重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">卜永柱：</span></b><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1976</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日出生，本名卜永梓，广东省湛江市人，湛江市遂溪县洋青镇老深村<span lang="EN-US">42</span>号居民，自由职业者，维权公民，南方街头运动践行者，人权捍卫者，中国在押政治犯。多年来，一直从事南方街头运动，积极参与各种维权互动；曾声援被当局超期羁押和被枉法抓判的民主维权公民“屠夫”吴淦、“南方老头”黄永祥和王远东等；曾围观人权活动人士李明哲案、“李小玲<span lang="EN-US">64</span>光明行案”和人权律师谢阳案庭审等；曾多次参加对八九六四事件的纪念活动；正是基于以上行为，遂其多次遭到广东省湛江市的强烈打压；<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，六四敏感日前夕，曾因与朋友穿着纪念六四的文化衫在广东街头拍照，而遭当地国保警方约谈，追问其在六四会有什么活动，其称“与朋友拍照纪念六四周年，是希望下一代知道有六四事件”；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，曾因转发广东公民刘兵上街举牌呼吁民众六四上街游行而被扣的消息，遂被广东省东莞市派出所警方以“扰乱社会秩序罪”为由强行带走传唤数小时，问及有关刘兵为六四举牌的相关事宜，以及其有否接受外媒采访等；同年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，曾因前往湖南省长沙市与他人一切围观谢阳案，但当返回东莞时，发现其工作了<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年的公司竟将其解雇，并要求其尽快离开；同年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，又因到北京协助并参与“李小玲<span lang="EN-US">64</span>光明行”而被北京警方以涉嫌”寻衅滋事罪”刑拘，一个月后被取保释放；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，其离开湛江市老家想要前往珠三角地区访友，并随便寻找合适的工作，而被遂溪县警方以“寻衅滋事”为由处行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">5</span>天；同年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，因在微信朋友圈里转发有关博鳌亚洲论坛的段子，两天后旋即被广东省遂溪县警方以“散布谣言”为由处行政拘留<span lang="EN-US">10</span>天；获释后，为讨公道，其对遂溪县警方对其所做的违宪违法行为提出了行政复议申请；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，因其朋友与人起纷争，其前去劝架而未果，后警方接到报警将在场<span lang="EN-US">6</span>人悉数带走盘查，次日其余人等均被释放，而其则被当地国保警方带走刑拘，罪名疑似“寻衅滋事”；后其被湛江市遂溪县检察院予以正式批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，据悉，其案已被湛江市遂溪县法院秘密庭审，有几位朋友前去法院要求旁听，法院既不让进入亦不告知其任何信息；截至当前，其最终被判几年，暂无人知晓；据悉，因其被抓捕判刑，其家属生活陷入窘况，其妻子既要看顾两个年幼的孩子，又要照顾其年老公婆和身患疾病无法工作的大哥。</span><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2022</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日获悉卜永柱最终被中共当局判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">曲红、</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font:
