mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">曲永霞</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">齐红玉：</span></b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">黑龙江省双鸭山市集贤县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日<span lang="EN-US">10</span>点左右，集贤县法轮功学员齐红玉女士在街上讲真相时，被不明真相世人诬告，被抓捕到前进派出所。下午三点多，国保大队长冯树斌等人，带着开锁人员打开齐红玉家门抄家，当晚把齐红玉送进双鸭山市看守所。后在未通知家人的情况下，集贤县法院非法对齐红玉开庭，判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年有期徒刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">齐文伯<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"> </span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">天津市武清区豆张庄镇周立营村法轮功学员<span lang="EN-US">,</span>女，<span lang="EN-US">1962</span>年生。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，李保兰、齐文伯在发放法轮功资料时被豆张庄镇派出所警察抓捕并抄家。由于身体原因（血压高），她们被以取保候审的名义放回家中。但<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年多来，公检法相关人员一直在构陷她们。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日左右，李保兰、齐文伯先后被开庭。李保兰被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，齐文伯被判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，但在庭审判决后她们安全回家了。可在<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，她们被豆张庄派出所警察与法院执行庭的人，强行从家中抓捕到武清看守所关押。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="http://www.minghui.tv/mh/articles/2022/11/25/%E5%A4%A9%E6%B4%A5%E5%B8%82%E4%B8%A4%E4%BD%8D%E8%80%81%E5%B9%B4%E5%A6%87%E5%A5%B3%E6%9D%8E%E4%BF%9D%E5%85%B0%E3%80%81%E9%BD%90%E6%96%87%E4%BC%AF%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91-452342.html"><b face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">齐小云：</span></b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">河南平顶山市法轮功学员，</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1973</span>年生，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日傍晚，在家中被光明路派出所抄家、抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月获悉齐小云被判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/10/11/450645.html#22101022421-5"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span color="windowtext" face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/10/11/450645.html#22101022421-5</span></b></a></span><b><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">戚凤珍：</span></b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吉林白城市法轮功学员，女。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日发放法轮功资料，被白城市公安局抓捕，被关押在白城市看守所。看守所不让家属见面，家属担忧戚凤珍的身体情况。在被非法关押、被构陷大半年后，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年过年前夕，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。戚凤珍刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">恰特合·达吾列提（哈）：</span></b><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1988</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日出生，新疆维吾尔自治区伊犁哈萨克斯坦自治州人，伊犁哈萨克斯坦自治州察布查尔锡伯自治县捷仁布拉克镇<span lang="EN-US">67</span>团<span lang="EN-US">8</span>连哈萨克族公民，中国在押良心犯。被抓捕前，一直是遵纪守法的好公民，并因身有严重疾患长期与病魔做着殊死搏斗；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，曾被新疆建设兵团农四师医院诊断为慢性粒细胞白血病；后因病情严重，于<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日被转到新疆医科大学第一附属医院住院治疗<span lang="EN-US">8</span>天；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年，曾两度前往北京市住院治疗，但又因无力承担高昂的治疗费用<span lang="EN-US">,</span>只能中途放弃治疗；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，其病情再次复发，不得不在新疆医科大学第一附属医院住院治疗，每月药费<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，恰特合·达吾列提被伊犁州察布查尔锡伯自治县警方突然以不明罪由抓捕，被送入当地“教育培训中心”（又称“再教育营”）接受中共洗脑式教育；同年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，旋即被察布查尔锡伯自治县检察院予以批捕；<span lang="EN-US"> 2019</span>年，被伊犁哈萨克斯坦自治州察布查尔锡伯自治县法院以不明罪名重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">19</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2037</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日； 据悉，其被判刑前因身患白血病严重，医生建议做干细胞移植手术，但向狱方申请保外就医以求手术治疗，遭拒；又悉，因其被抓捕判刑，其家人（妻子、两个孩子及其母亲）生活陷入困境。目前疑似在新疆伊犁哈萨克斯坦自治州新源监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">强巴格勒</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">（藏）</span></b><b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：</span></b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">四川省甘孜藏族羌族自治区州阿坝县尼措寺僧人，<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">23</span>岁，是道孚县人。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日傍晚<span lang="EN-US">8</span>点多钟，强巴格勒在前往附近一佛塔转经途中，突然被中共公安人员拘捕。被指在僧舍中挂有西藏国旗，并曾表露想要为西藏政教事业而自焚的念头。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">强巴旺秋（藏）</span></b><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">:1959</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年出生，西藏自治区边波隆都县索托乡（注：此为藏语拼音名，汉语地名不明，疑为拉萨市附近某县<span lang="EN-US">/</span>乡）人，藏名<span lang="EN-US">Jampel Wangchuk</span>，俗名次培（<span lang="EN-US">Tsephel</span>），拉萨市哲蚌寺洛色林僧院高级僧人、纪律纠察僧官，学者僧侣，中国在押良心犯。自幼成为僧侣，并在西藏拉萨市哲蚌寺所在僧侣学院进修学习；后因长期师从藏族著名佛学教师兰林仁波切（<span lang="EN-US">Lamrim<span style="mso-spacerun: yes;">&nbsp; </span>Rinpoche</span>），成为其身边主要弟子，随拥有深厚博学的藏传佛学知识，且被哲蚌寺洛色林僧院确定为高级僧人及纪律纠察僧官；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，西藏发生大规模以僧侣为主体的抗议示威活动，以表达对中共当局长期压制、管控藏区人民的不满；他们强烈呼吁中共当局要实现（或兑现）藏民族“自治独立”，并要求让达赖喇嘛回国返乡，对藏区进行自治管理等政治诉求；针对此，同年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，拉萨的哲蚌寺约有<span lang="EN-US">350</span>名僧侣亦本着推动实现这些诉求，发起进一步的大规模抗议活动，使事态迅速波及到整个拉萨市区，甚至四川及青海藏区；对于此次抗议行动，中共警方随即采取了制止行为，但又因中共手段过于极端，导致双方发生对峙冲突，期间部分僧人被抓；<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，其被拉萨市警方突然以涉嫌“抗议活动”刑拘，自此失联；另有同寺僧侣好友贡觉尼玛、阿旺觉尼亦被拘捕；后其被拉萨市警方正式逮捕，理由是虽未参加当时的抗议示威，但因未能阻止所在寺庙僧人举行大规模抗议行动，遂属于违规或违反相关管理条例行为；<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，在超期关押<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年之久后，终被拉萨市中级法院秘密重判无期徒刑，罪名不详；据悉，其辩护权遭剥夺，至今其在狱中健康状况及所处具体环境等均无下落。目前疑似在拉萨曲水监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">乔向阳：</span></b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">河南新郑市法轮功信徒、残疾人。家住新郑市龙湖镇沙窝李村，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日下午被新郑市警方以“扫黑除恶”的名义抓捕，家中私人物品被掠走。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，新郑市法院对乔向阳判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">乔鑫鑫</span></b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：本名杨泽伟，<span lang="EN-US">1986</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月出生，湖南省祁东县人，客居老挝中国公民，新闻媒体人，前广州市某新闻媒体职员，前自由亚洲电台驻东南亚特约记者，中国拆墙运动（<span lang="EN-US">BanGFW</span>）发起人，“拆墙宝典”写作和推动者，海外民主派人士，中国在押政治犯。大学时期，曾因看到长达<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个小时的六四大屠杀影片而深感震撼，故自此频繁接触美国人，并在一家驻华美国文化中心作兼职人员，以了解和体悟到中国宣传的虚假与邪恶；大学毕业后，曾因到广东省广州市做新闻工作者，故而积极利用职业之便经常在美国总领事馆参加文化讲座活动；曾参加<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年美国总统大选观摩会和，并阅览一年香港英文日报，使自己知晓更多与中国官方新闻报导相左的信息，并深切体会、感悟到新闻真实性报导的重要性；曾因中共自<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年代末起开始建起网络长城防火墙（<span lang="EN-US">Great Firewall</span>，简称：<span lang="EN-US">GFW</span>），实行互联网边界网络审查系统，而使其在中国境内使用手机和计算机时深感防火墙给其及国人阅览设限带来的困扰；后其移居老挝生活，并学习了十种语言；曾因中国逐渐成为世界最大的电子监狱，为了维稳不惜每年花费巨<span lang="EN-US">60</span>亿美元打造网络防火墙，封锁了<span lang="EN-US">Google</span>、<span lang="EN-US">Twitter</span>、<span lang="EN-US">Youtube</span>、<span lang="EN-US">BBC</span>、<span lang="EN-US">CNN</span>等全球<span lang="EN-US">31</span>万个网站，造成国人只能接触中共的洗脑讯息，而且，近年来因中国将防火墙技术输出到俄罗斯、伊朗、缅甸、柬埔寨等国，迫使十几亿人每天无端地去仇美、反日、攻台，造成了全球冲突连绵不断，遂其据此开始致力于把新兴的拆墙运动（<span lang="EN-US">BanGFW</span>）理念向多国推广，呼吁大家都来举牌、发帖；<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，其等海外民主派人士发起拆墙运动，并推出《拆墙宝典》，争取国际社会各方支持，以期达到将中共主管建立和运作防火墙的首要份子提交海牙国际刑事法院的要求；<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日获悉，其六四<span lang="EN-US">34</span>周年纪念日前夕的<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，突遭中国警方跨境抓捕；后知其在当地侨领、老挝警方的连手配合下被中国警方野蛮绑架，自此失联，至今下落不明。目前被羁押地点缺详。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/06/blog-post_17.html"><b><span color="windowtext" face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/06/blog-post_17.html</span></b></a></span><b><u><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">秦红英：</span></b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">江西<span lang="EN-US">9</span>江市法轮功学员。秦红英<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日贴法轮功不干胶，遭甘棠派出所抓捕，被关押在<span lang="EN-US">9</span>江市沙河县看守所。后获悉，秦红英被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，关押在江西女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/11/25/%E6%B1%9F%E8%A5%BF%E4%B9%9D%E6%B1%9F%E5%B8%82%E7%A7%A6%E7%BA%A2%E8%8B%B1%E5%B7%B2%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4%E5%85%A5%E7%8B%B1-434008.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span color="windowtext" face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/11/25/%E6%B1%9F%E8%A5%BF%E4%B9%9D%E6%B1%9F%E5%B8%82%E7%A7%A6%E7%BA%A2%E8%8B%B1%E5%B7%B2%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4%E5%85%A5%E7%8B%B1-434008.html</span></b></a></span><b><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">秦丽杰：</span></b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">陕西宝鸡石油机械厂法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日下午，宝鸡市金台公安分局出动了多辆警车、几十个警察，抓捕了宝鸡石油机械厂的八名法轮功学员及家属。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，秦丽杰、李宝莲、寇爱梅三人被关押到宝鸡第二看守所非法逮捕、关押，其他人已于<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日被释放回家。后获悉秦丽杰被判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，寇爱梅被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年半，李宝莲被判<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月。秦丽杰刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">秦少华</span></b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">：山东省潍坊市高密市法轮功学员，女，高密市夏庄镇益民村人，一九九八年和家人一起开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月中共迫害法轮功后，秦少华一家人频频遭迫害，父母曾被判刑，秦少华也曾被劳教。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日秦少华再次被高密市孚日派出所警察抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月得知，她已被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。从开庭到判刑都没有通知家属。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 11pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/7/20/463179.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span color="windowtext" face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/7/20/463179.html</span></b></a></span><b><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">秦泗枫：</span></b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">北京市人，基督徒，北京市灯台基督教家庭教会牧师，中国在押良心犯。笃信耶稣基督，并一直在教会里做神职人员，传讲基督教福音，并积极鼓励和身体力行做差传事工（即因循广传基督教福音的原则和使命，在教会自身工作之外，以人力、物力、财力及祷告等向外——主指到本国其他地区或外国从事福音工作，并建立教会等）活动；但因其所在北京市灯台基督教会属归正家庭教会，不愿配合接受中共“三自”教会的管辖，遂自新宗教事务条例实施以来，即成为被中共当局欲加逼迫打压的家庭教会之一；在此期间，其及教会同工、众教友（信众）均因基督教信仰问题以及对外差传事工行为而深受地方政府的密切关注与打压；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月：当其与教会同工苏民军女士以教会名义在云南省进行差传宣教活动时，被山东省淄博市警方突然跨境抓捕；同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，又被淄博市检察院以涉嫌“非法经营罪”转正式批捕，控其因为教会印刷了一些赞美诗的歌本，虽只在教会内部使用，但其行为触犯了中共当局的宗教事务管理条例，故而应予逮捕法办；截至当前，除了知其二人各自家属对他们被抓捕十分担忧，并呼吁教会信徒为其平安和坚固信心而代祷之外，其个人后续情况鲜为人知。目前被羁押于山东省淄博市看守所（山东省淄博市张店区傅家镇傅家村，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">255063</span>）。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/11/blog-post_5.html"><b><span color="windowtext" face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/11/blog-post_5.html</span></b></a></span><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b><span color="windowtext" face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">秦小坡：</span></b><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1982</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日出生，北京市人，北京市昌平区东小口镇公民，清华大学毕业生，个人投资者，抗强拆维权者，中国在押维权人士。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，北京市昌平区东小口镇政府进行“旧村改造”，欲对基层辖区马连店村进行强拆，其父母秦荣、高和平因是该村村民，夫妻二人的宅基地和住房列强拆范围；此非法强拆决定立遭到其父母及其家人、同村其他村民一致反对，其父母二人于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日两次向北京市昌平区政府申请行政复议；后经昌平区政府复议，决定“撤销东小口镇政府的限拆和强拆决定，且此后政府将重新启动”对其父母房屋的强拆工作；对此处置决定，其父母及其本人均认为有失公允和法理，故不断投诉控告，以期寻求公平正义；为快速了解此事，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日、<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，北京市昌平区警方决定向其父母出具《不予调查处理告知书》，拒绝调查处理；此处理方式明显有警方的渎职行为和消极纵容马连店村委和合作社违法犯罪的行为，遂双方发生更深争议，并在之后的强拆行动中双方发生了激烈冲突；期间，马连店村委和合作社曾多次组织专门人马对其父母及其本人进行暴力威胁和殴打等，试图用单方制定的安置补偿方案强迫其父母接受；最终其父母民宅仍然在未达成安置补偿协议的前提下，被强行推毁和强占；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，其出于保护父母房屋所有权，在阻抗强拆时曾手持过二踢脚鞭炮，以求正当防卫，然而却遭对方陷害，在强拆行为结束后，当地政府仍派多人上门骚扰、威吓和殴打其全家人，使其及其母亲均遭暴力伤害，尤其是其被严重打伤，住进住院，伤势不明；后其被派出所警方抓走，并被北京市昌平区警方以非法持有爆炸物为罪由监视居住于昌平区小汤山医院住院（治疗）<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月，监视居住期满日，其被以涉嫌“持有爆炸物罪”转为刑拘；同年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，又被北京市昌平区检察院更换罪名，以涉嫌“爆炸罪”予以批捕。目前被羁押于北京市昌平区看守所（北京市昌平区南口镇曹庄村，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">102202</span>）。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/03/blog-post_19.html"><b><span color="windowtext" face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">重庆法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">4</span>千元。张盛全、李嘉惠，被枉判<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，勒索罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元；李玉华<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">8</span>千元，监外执行；高洪伟<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元；秦雪美刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: 0pt;">秦亚莉：</span></b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1947</span>年生，中国电子信息产业集团有限公司会计师。山西太原法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月被抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，秦亚莉被太原迎泽法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。现秦亚莉被关押古交第四女子看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/12/4/452684.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span color="windowtext" face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; class="MsoNormal"><b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">秦燕：</span></b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">江苏省南通市维权人士。江苏省南通市崇川区唐闸街道新园村二组<span lang="EN-US">4</span>号居民。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日秦燕被抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月底，律师曾会见了秦燕，秦燕坚信自己是无罪的，她告知，警方抓她和她的举报视频得罪了当地公安有关。该举报视频显示：<span lang="EN-US"> 2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，南通市崇川分局出动了几十名警察和辅警，在无任何违法事实的情况下，捏造事实伪造证据，将在秦燕家吃饭的十四名亲友，全部以涉嫌赌博的名义传唤，非法限制人身自由达八小时以上。因事发突然，导致秦燕父亲当场被吓瘫在地，后送往医院进行急救，但落下了严重的忧郁症，虽经多次住院治疗，但至今未获痊愈。在视频最后，秦燕还上传了自己的控告信，署名时间为<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日。而就在上述举报视频发布后不久，秦燕于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>号在平潮的婆家家中，被南通崇川区治安大队带走，并以秦燕涉嫌寻衅滋事罪对南通市城区家里，和店铺进行了搜查，并查扣了电脑、移动电话等电子用品。当天，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日秦燕被如皋市公安局指定监视居住在如皋白浦。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2023</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日秦燕因举报公安而被控寻衅滋事案于在南通看守所第二驻所法庭开庭审理。未宣判。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/04/2023424.html"><b><span color="windowtext" face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/04/2023424.html</span></b></a></span><b><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">秦永敏：</span></b><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">1953</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日出生，湖北省鄂州市籍人，早年为湖北省武汉钢铁公司冷轧厂职工，著名民间政治学者、自由撰稿人，中国民主党湖北省党部重要创始人，“中国人权观察”理事长、“玫瑰中国团队”负责人，著名人权活动家，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日，其被湖北省当局再度非法抓捕，罪由是“接受外媒采访及写文章过多”，其妻亦遭当局拘押、失联；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日获悉，其已被湖北省武汉市警方以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”秘密羁押。现得知被羁押于武汉市第二看守所，案子在检察院。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日第一次获律师会见，状态良好。</span><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">2018</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日上午在武汉中级法院三号审判庭公开宣判。秦永敏被以颠覆政权罪判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期自<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日起至<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日止。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">覃秋艳（妮可）：</span></b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1979</span>年出生，广西壮族自治区柳州市籍人，香港新移民，香港身份证英文名：妮可，常用推特账户名：<span lang="EN-US">@Hk60740379Hk</span>，南方公民行动和公民聚会参与者，香港“返送中”运动参与者，香港、广州、深圳三地人权活动者，中国在押政治犯。早年曾在广东省深圳市生活，曾多次参与深圳等地的公民行动与公民聚会，并对生活贫困的公民有过资助；自<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月起，开始移民香港，并获得香港公民身份；曾因关注中国的人权状况而穿梭活跃于香港与内地的广州、深圳等城市，故而曾在广东省惠州市惠阳区办事时遭到中国秘密警察的跟踪；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，曾因支持港人对香港选举要求“真普选”，而积极参加了香港的“占中”运动；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年，曾因全身心投入香港的“反修例”运动，而经常在香港的街头进行站台宣传与抗议；同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，曾因原广州维权人士廖剑豪（现已定居香港）在香港铜锣湾东角道被港警烟雾弹击中，正在附近街头作采访节目的她随即加入对其的营救，并对其眼、口等处予以及时清洁；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，因其母亲<span lang="EN-US">80</span>岁生日将至，其随返回内地深圳市，准备在疫情所致的“宾馆隔离”<span lang="EN-US">14</span>天后赶回老家广西柳州，不料却在解除隔离日（即<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日），被中国警方秘密抓捕，自此失联；后经友人多方查询打探，同年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，知其已被广西壮族自治区柳州市警方拘捕，涉嫌罪名不清；据悉，其此次被抓疑与其在香港参加反送中运动，且频繁将运动实时信息发于推特之上有关；截至当前，其已被超期关押近<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年，并因其家人恐受威胁而拒透其具体信息，故而友人对其的发声呼吁一直未引起国内外媒体的关注。</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">后被以煽动颠覆国家政权罪判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年。目前疑似被羁押于柳州市看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/05/6.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span color="windowtext" face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/05/6.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">覃永沛：</span></b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">广西人权律师。覃永沛是在<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月被注销律师牌照。由他主持，曾代理过不少维权案件的”百举鸣律师事务所”，被勒令解散后，转为法律咨询公司的形式，继续提供法律服务。覃永沛也连同多名维权律师，成立“中国律师后俱乐部”。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月末，覃永沛所属原律师事务所律师陈家鸿被玉林警方拘留，罪名为“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”。当时覃永沛曾积极作出声援及呼吁放人，目前陈家鸿律师尚在羁押。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日傍晚五点左右，南宁警方十数人闯入原百举鸣律师事务所（现百永鸣法律咨询服务有限公司）办公室，将该所原主任、人权律师后覃永沛控制并带走，同时覃的办公室被警方查封。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，广西人权律师覃永沛被指涉煽动颠覆国家政权罪遭刑事拘留。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月案件移送检察院审查起诉。已经进入审判阶段，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日开庭。现关押在南宁第二看守所。</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">覃永沛案被最高法院于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日决定再延期<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月，广西南宁中院<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日才通知律师。此前，覃永沛律师妻子也是其代理辩护人于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>号寄了取保候审申请书后到现在，准或不准，没有任何通知，法律明文规定三日之内作出书面答复的。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，广西人权律师覃永沛煽动颠覆国家政权案一审宣判，判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，刑期从<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日起至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日止。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><a name="_Hlk109582210"></a><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/03/5_31.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk109582210;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span color="windowtext" face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/03/5_31.html</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk109582210;"></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk109582210;"><b mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk109582210;"><b><u><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">卿立菊：</span></u></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk109582210;"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">四川省彭州市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1971</span>年生，家住四川省彭州市蒙阳镇三湾村。她曾于<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月遭抓捕后被中共法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日上午<span lang="EN-US">9</span>点多，卿立菊和法轮功学员付顺菊在蒙阳镇物流市场向世人赠送法轮功<span lang="EN-US">U</span>盘时，被抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日晚<span lang="EN-US">6</span>点多，卿立菊被蒙阳派出所警察戴上黑头套劫往新津洗脑班迫害。卿立菊于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日被彭州法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，现已被转入四川邛崃监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/16/446305.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk109582210;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/7/16/446305.html</span></b></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk109582210;"></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt;">仇运凤：</span></b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt;">湖北省荆州市荆州区法轮功学员。荆州市荆州区法轮功学员王美卿、刘新安、仇运凤、邓永梅<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日晚上，开着汽车在马山（荆州与当阳、枝江交界处）发放法轮功资料时、被人举报，被当阳市（属湖北宜昌市管辖）草埠湖派出所警察抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日当阳市法院下达了判决书：仇运凤被判处<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元；王美卿被判处<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">6</span>千元；刘新安被判处<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>个月，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">5</span>千元；邓咏梅被判处<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">2</span>千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/10/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E5%8D%81%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-436647.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span color="windowtext" face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/10/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E5%8D%81%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-436647.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">曲红：</span></b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">山西太原公民、网络活跃人士，网名婷婷。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日遭太原警方以涉嫌寻衅滋事为由刑事拘留，目前关押在太原第三看守所。著名媒体人潇男女士介绍说：婷婷参与了微信群不计其数的公益讲座转播，她为中国民间社群的思想交流，奉献了上千个日夜，她勤勉、低调、勇敢，她是最富志愿者精神的网络义工之一。后信息全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">曲嘉旺波：</span></b><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1973</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，藏族名<span lang="EN-US">ChoegyalWangpo</span>，西藏自治区日喀则市定日县扎那村人，日喀则市定日县协格尔镇查那村当卓寺（藏人称之为登卓寺（<span lang="EN-US">Tengdro</span>））僧人，慈善公益捐助人，中国在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">-9</span>月，曾因到西藏首府拉萨市做佛事访问时，误将手机丢在一家咖啡馆，老板随将手机交给当地警方希望帮助查找失主；孰料拉萨市警方在翻查手机时，查出其与尼泊尔的多名同乡藏僧有联系或拥有和达赖喇嘛有关照片或文献，并有捐款帮助<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月尼泊尔大地震当地的藏人及寺院、小区重建等记录，随引起中共西藏当局的极大不快和恐慌；同年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，其家乡扎那村和毗邻的当卓寺遭到日喀则市当局派出的多名武警和公安警察的夜袭，所有僧人及村民被强迫接受政治洗脑教育，多人被殴打，包含其在内的<span lang="EN-US">20</span>僧侣被拘留，所在区域的网络连接被切断；<span lang="EN-US">3</span>天后，一名僧人因向当局抗议而被自杀，其余僧人均被超押数月不予释放；后其与另<span lang="EN-US">3</span>名藏僧被日喀则市警方以涉嫌“跟境外藏人联系、赈济尼泊尔地震，或拥有和达赖喇嘛有关照片或文献”为罪由转正式逮捕，自此失联；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日获悉，其一行<span lang="EN-US">4</span>人案在日喀则中级法院庭审，最终被以“危害国家安全罪”判处<span lang="EN-US">20</span>年<span lang="EN-US">-5</span>年不等刑期；其中，其被判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">20</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2039</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月。目前疑似在拉萨市札基监狱服刑。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/06/20.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span color="windowtext" face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/06/20.html</span></b></a></span><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">曲桑嘉措（藏）：</span></b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">青海省海南藏族自治州安多茫拉县鲁仓寺僧人曲桑嘉措，带领当地一民间组织，长期向农牧民们提供藏文化教育方面的帮助。他于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日遭中共当局拘捕，至今下落不明。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月底曲桑嘉措就曾因他所撰写的一些文章内容，而遭当局拘押<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个多月，此次遭捕，他的家属仍未被告知他的被捕原因。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">曲兴：</span></b><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">1989</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年出生，原籍辽宁省沈阳市，四川省成都市长居公民，自由职业者，原为一心想出家的寻法人（即想当僧侣），后成为法轮功修炼者和信仰者，中国在押良心犯。早期曾一度想当僧侣，故四处游历寺庙学习经法，并专程到西藏学习藏传佛教和出境到尼泊尔师从著名法师，然而一直未能如愿；后其在尼泊尔修行时在网上发现并购得一本法轮功书籍，自此立定心志，决定回国研读法轮功；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年，其选择四川省成都市作为居住地，自此成为一名法轮功修炼者；但因积极向他人推介法轮功的讯息与功效，遂遭成都市当局的维稳打压；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，因其在送外卖时黏贴了法轮功讯息的不干胶，遂其及与其同住的母亲当天即被成都市高新区肖家河派出所警方非法抓走，租住屋遭查抄；后其母亲被监视居住，<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月后被行政处罚<span lang="EN-US">900</span>元，而其却被成都市高新区警方以涉嫌“邪教罪”刑拘、逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，其案被高新区检察院提起公诉，并移交到高新区法院审查；<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，在被超期关押<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年半后，终被四川省成都市高新区法院以“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元；刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。曲兴一审被成判八年，上诉至成都市中院后，被维持一审原判。原被羁押于成都市看守所（成都市郫都区安靖镇正义路<span lang="EN-US">3</span>号，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">611731</span>）。目前曲兴已经被转入到四川乐山嘉州监狱。</span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/7/7/462735.html<o:p></o:p></span></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/2/20/456953.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span color="windowtext" face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/2/20/456953.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/04/8.html"><b><span color="windowtext" face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/04/8.html</span></b></a></span><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b><span color="windowtext" face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">曲永霞：</span></b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江省黑河市孙吴县法轮功学员，女。</span><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2022</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日上午，孙吴县国保杜森带领孙吴县东派出所和社区的一些人员闯入曲永霞家中，抓捕了曲永霞，并且搜查，抄走家中修炼用的大法书籍和笔记本电脑。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，曲永霞被黑河市爱辉区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/6/6/461669.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span color="windowtext" face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/6/6/461669.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 22pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">R</span></b><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">.<o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">热依拉•达吾提（维吾尔）、</span><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">任桂芬、</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">任海飞、任惠萍、任召军、任胜林、任素香、</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">任秀兰</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、任志强、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">仁青持真</span><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">日赛（藏）、<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">荣铁文</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">、荣西（藏）、</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">肉孜•艾木杜拉（维）、</span><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">如凯•嘎玛桑珠（藏）、</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">阮晓寰</span><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">热依拉·达吾提（维吾尔）：</span></b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女、<span lang="EN-US">1966</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日出生，新疆乌鲁木齐市人，维吾尔族，维族名<span lang="EN-US">Rahile Dawut</span>（ </span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">راھىلە</span><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> </span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">داۋۇت</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">），乌鲁木齐市天山区胜利路街道新疆大学小区居民，中共党员，新疆大学中文系教授，新疆大学少数民族民俗研究中心主任、教授及少数民族语言文学方向硕士研究生导师，国际知名维吾尔民俗与民族志专家、人类学家，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">1983</span>年—<span lang="EN-US">1987</span>年就读于新疆大学中文系维吾尔语言文学专业，毕业时获学士学位，后又于<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月在新疆大学中文系获得少数民族民间文学（含民俗学）专业硕士学位、<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月在北京师范大学中文系获得民俗学博士学位；自<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月以来，一直在新疆大学中文系任教；期间，因创建、领导了新疆大学少数民族民俗研究中心，并在国际期刊和许多书籍上撰写了数十篇文章（含对中亚伊斯兰圣地的研究，并在世界各地的会议上展示其工作），曾屡受国内与国际学术界认可；曾多次在美国宾西法尼亚大学民俗学系、美国印第安纳大学及美国加利福尼亚大学作访问学者和访问教授；曾在新疆大学培养研究生<span lang="EN-US">18</span>人，已毕业研究生<span lang="EN-US">12</span>人；<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，其因接到一通单位领导的电话，要求其收拾行李尽快到北京参加一个紧急会议，其随后即匆匆出门，赶赴机场，不想却在前往北京的旅途中失去联系，自此音讯全无；后经其女儿（当时已在国外）等家人的四处打探和国际呼吁，终知其已于同期与其他多位维吾尔知识分子和文化精英一起被新疆当局刑事拘留；后其被乌鲁木齐市警方以涉嫌“分裂主义”罪由转正式逮捕，指控其利用研究课题在农民和政府之间造成了社会“挑衅”；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，被中共新疆当局以“民族分裂主义罪”等秘判有期徒刑，刑期不详；据悉，因其在狱中遭受酷刑或心理压力，其身体健康出现严重问题。目前疑似在新疆乌鲁木齐市一家监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/12/blog-post_16.html"><b><span color="windowtext" face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2021/12/blog-post_16.html</span></b></a></span><b><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">任桂芬：</span></b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">辽宁</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">本溪市法轮功学员，女。李洪军和任桂芬夫妇因为修炼法轮大法，信仰真善忍，丈夫李洪军曾被判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年、任桂芬曾被判刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，任桂芬和丈夫李洪军，及姐姐任桂娥和妹妹遭本溪市明山区公安分局、卧龙派出所警察抓捕。妹妹随后回家。任桂芬和姐姐任桂娥被关押到本溪看守所。任桂芬后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日，她被关押到辽宁省女子监狱，现被关押在十二监区（即集训矫治监区）。辽宁省女子监狱通知家属，称不许存钱、接见。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/11/20/452137.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span color="windowtext" face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/11/20/452137.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt;">任海飞：</span></b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt;">辽宁省大连市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，任海飞在自己所租住的钻石湾寓所，被大连市公安局甘井子区分局国保大队和甘井子街派出所警察抓捕并抄家，抢走逾<span lang="EN-US">55</span>万元现金，以及价值<span lang="EN-US">20</span>多万元的存储卡等电子产品。同时被抓捕的还有大连市法轮功学员孙中丽。任海飞、孙中丽被关押构陷一年多后，于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日宣判，任海飞被判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年并罚款十万元。孙中丽被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年、罚款七万元。他们都已上诉。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月初被告知，不开庭维持原判。任海飞刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2030</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/17/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%83%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-436935.html#22116224158-1"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span color="windowtext" face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/17/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%83%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-436935.html#22116224158-1</span></b></a></span><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">任惠萍<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;"> </span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">云南玉溪市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日任惠萍发法轮功真相资料，被绑架到红塔分局。当天深夜十一点多，玉溪市红塔分局国保大队到任惠萍家，抄家，警察以打印机是她女儿张亢的为借口，在凌晨一点多，抓捕了张亢及抢走家里的私人物品。任惠萍、张亢母女俩被非法关押在红塔区看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日被玉溪市江川县法院视频开庭，<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日任惠萍、张亢母女均被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。任惠萍刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">任召军</span></b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：河南省济源市法轮功学员。男，<span lang="EN-US">1988</span>年生，河南省济源市轵城镇西留养村人。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，济源市公安局“<span lang="EN-US">610</span>”警察李建锋带领多人使用梯子翻墙跳入任召军家的院内后，又破门闯入任召军的房内，翻箱倒柜，抄走了电脑、打印机、手机、银行卡、银行存折、大法书籍以及其它部份财物等<span lang="EN-US">34</span>件，又绑抓捕了任召军及父母一家三人到济源市看守所。一个月后，父亲任宗禄被“取保候审”回家。任召军和王庆英被济源市检察院起诉。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，济源市法院宣布判任召军<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年刑期并且罚款二万五千元，判王庆英<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月刑期并且罚款六千元。随后，任召军和母亲王庆英均上诉到济源市中级法院，但均被驳回，维持非法原判。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，王庆英被遣送到河南省女子监狱，任召军仍然被非法关押在河南省济源市看守所。任召军刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">任胜林：</span></b><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">60</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">多岁，四川省德阳市人，原德阳市什邡市钻釆厂退休工人，法轮功信仰者、良心犯。因信仰和宣传法轮功而长期受到什邡市当局的监控打压。<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日被四川省什邡市回澜镇派出所警方突击传唤，并被非法送到什邡市拘留所拘留<span lang="EN-US">15</span>天。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日上午<span lang="EN-US">9</span>点，再次被便衣警察非法绑架，其家被查抄，搜走大量有关法轮功书籍和资料宣传品，后被以涉嫌“邪教罪”刑拘和逮捕。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，他被什邡市法院一审以“组织实施邪教罪”判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。目前仍被关押在德阳市公安局监管中心。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">任素香：</span></b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">内蒙古赤峰市元宝山区元宝山镇南庙村法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年五十五岁。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日上午，赤峰市元宝山区公安局多个警察非法闯入任素香的家，抢走打印机、电脑、现金等私人物品。当时任素香到邻居家，警察追到邻居家将她抓捕。任素香被关押在元宝山区看守所。在这没有任何法律程序的情况下，任素香被构陷到法院。法院指派的律师不仅不维护任素香的权利，还威胁任素香与她家人。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日任素香被判刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">任秀兰：</span></b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁省营口市法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1950</span>年生，家住营口市鱍鱼圈区，<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，任秀兰在自己居住的小区里向邻居讲述法轮功真相，遭不明真相的吴姓居民构陷，被鱍鱼圈区国保警察抓捕到红旗派出所，警察抢走任秀兰家门钥匙，五个警察拿着钥匙到任秀兰家抄家，抢走法轮功书籍、真相资料和现金等私人财物；后来任秀兰被关押到营口市看守所关押迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日被营口市站前区法院庭审，后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">任志强：</span></b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">著名退休企业家、公众人物。<span lang="EN-US">1951</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日生，绰号任大炮，男，籍贯山东莱州，中国企业家，历任北京市华远地产董事长、华远集团党委副书记兼董事长、北京市商业银行（北京银行前身）监事、新华保险董事。后退休。持有中国人民大学法律硕士学位。曾任北京市政协委员。父亲任泉生曾任商业部副部长。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，中共北京市纪律检查委员会、北京市监察委员会发布消息，称北京市华远集团原党委副书记、董事长任志强涉嫌严重违纪违法，目前正接受北京市西城区纪委区监委纪律审查和监察调查。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，北京市西城区纪委监察委发布通告，称任志强因严重违反共产党五项纪律，构成严重职务违法，涉嫌贪污、受贿、挪用公款、国有公司人员滥用职权犯罪，宣布开除任志强党籍处分，同时取消其的待遇，收缴违纪违法所得，涉嫌犯罪问题将移送检察机关依法审查起诉，所涉财物随案移送司法机关。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日上午九点三十分在北京市第二中级人民法院第九法庭开庭审理，任志强因言获罪被中共当局指控涉嫌贪污罪<span lang="EN-US">/</span>受贿罪<span lang="EN-US">/</span>挪用公款罪<span lang="EN-US">/</span>国有企业人员滥用职权罪等<span lang="EN-US">4</span>项罪。庭审中任志强一言不发，表达抗议。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，任志强被习近平当局判刑<span lang="EN-US">18</span>年，举世震惊。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">仁青持真：</span></b><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2019</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，仁青持真因涉嫌“煽动分裂国家罪”遭阿坝国家安全机关逮捕，时年<span lang="EN-US">29</span>岁。原因是在社交媒体上表达自己关于藏区政治和社会问题的想法，以及向朋友邮寄分享境外出版的“涉藏非法出版物”，当地国保曾因此警告他<span lang="EN-US">3</span>次。此外，仁青持真曾于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年在微信上与部分流亡藏人谈论“涉藏敏感话题”，而与他的弟弟诺日才让<span lang="EN-US">1</span>起被拘押过两次。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日是失踪班禅喇嘛更敦确吉尼玛的生日，当天他与海外朋友通话长达两个小时，全部通话内容被录音，成为当局拘捕他的理由之<span lang="EN-US">1</span>。当局还以非法撰写和发表涉藏敏感文章为由关闭了他经营多年的博客。仁青持真最后<span lang="EN-US">1</span>次用微信与印度的妹妹贡桑卓玛通话是在<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日；几天后，即<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日晚上他便遭到拘捕。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，当局传唤仁青的弟弟诺日才让了解仁青持真“涉嫌煽动分裂国家罪”的有关情况。后其被“煽动分裂国家罪”被判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日。拘押在四川省绵阳监狱。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">日赛（藏）：</span></b><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1983</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年出生，西藏自治区那曲地区比如县人，原比如镇孟庆村干部，政治异议人士，中国在押政治犯。自<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年以来，一直担任那曲地区比如镇孟庆村的村干部；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，因中共当局在其所在县各乡村展开‘爱国再教育运动’，并强迫藏民在各家屋顶上悬挂五星红旗，此举引起比如县农牧民、学生、僧人、尼姑、作家、歌手等各类人士的同声抗议，并发起连串示威活动，成为继<span lang="EN-US">2008</span>年后在西藏自治区内最大的示威抗议活动，随引发中共当局的极度恐惧，将比如县视为极不稳定地区，曾先后集结大批军警实施“维稳”，肆意拘捕僧俗藏人，对当地有影响力的藏人予以重判，并采取‘对内严厉打击示威民众，对外严密封锁消息’等措施；在此情况下，日赛所在孟庆村的藏民亦因参与了公开抗议与示威活动，遂遭致当局的严酷打压，于<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月被当地警方刑拘，并以涉嫌“参与抗议示威” 、“秘密组织相关人员在昂扎家里参加会议”等罪由被正式批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，被当地法院判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，具体罪名不详。目前在西藏自治区一家监狱服刑。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; tab-stops: 122.5pt; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">荣铁文：</span></b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">吉林市丰满区<span lang="EN-US">74</span>岁法轮功学员。女，<span lang="EN-US">1947</span>年生，曾为驾校当校长。<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年，荣铁文开始修炼法轮功。<b> </b><span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">曾遭多次迫害判刑。</span><span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月底，荣铁文在家再次被吉林市哈达弯派出所警察抓捕，关押在吉林市看守所。后来，她被吉林市丰满区法院判处<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月份被送往长春女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月底。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源</b>：</span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/26/2021-12-26.html#zip5"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span color="windowtext" face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/26/2021-12-26.html#zip5</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">荣西（藏）：</span></b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">青海果洛州玛多县扎陵湖乡河源新村村民，原籍为四川甘孜州德格县，现年<span lang="EN-US">29</span>岁，妻子名叫央吉，无子女。<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>号上午约<span lang="EN-US">10</span>点钟，桑珠与荣西、拉珍三人突然被四名来自玛多县城的公安人员拘捕。警方指控他们三人加入由境外藏人设立的不同微信组群中，通过语音通话讨论<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年西藏流亡社区大选。据悉他们三人目前被关押在玛多县人民法院里，但被禁止与其家属和亲友见面。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">肉孜•艾木杜拉（维）：</span></b><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1977</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年出生，新疆巴音郭楞蒙古自治州（简称巴音郭楞州）库尔勒市人，维吾尔族，穆斯林，成功民营企业家，房地产商人，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">-2019</span>年，因中共当局在新疆地区大规模抓捕维吾尔族、哈萨克斯坦族等少数族裔穆斯林，将他们送入新疆再教育营（被中共当局称为“职业技能教育培训中心”<span lang="EN-US">/</span>被新疆民间称为“转化所”、“学习班”<span lang="EN-US">/</span>被中国大陆媒体有时称为“去极端化培训班”、“教育转化培训中心”<span lang="EN-US"> /</span>被国际媒体和组织称为“集中营”、“拘留营”），并通过强化培训而将他们区分为普级、严级和强级三个等级，其中普级表明该人培训后即可释放回家，强级表明该人是死硬派，因不愿服从或配合当局洗脑教育，遂将被转逮捕、重判入监；在此情势下，其因自家弟兄姐妹等家人经常出入境外学习、生活和经商等，遂于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月亦被新疆库尔勒市当局作为“反恐反极端”维稳对象强行送进当地一所再教育营；后因其反对当局对维吾尔人的极端教育洗脑行为（主指意识上绝对服从中共领导，改变固有的民族信仰、接受无神论思想，进行汉化教育及饮食非清真食品等习惯），遂被库尔勒市警方以“去极端化”为由转为逮捕，同时，其及其弟在库尔勒市的大厦和三家餐厅被查封，自此失联；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，知其被新疆巴音郭楞蒙古自治州库尔勒市法院以疑似“煽动民族仇恨罪”等重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">25</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2042</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月；据悉，其两个姐姐亦遭抓捕，至今生死不明。目前疑似在新疆库尔勒监狱服刑。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/02/25.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span color="windowtext" face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/02/25.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">如凯•嘎玛桑珠（藏）：</span></b><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1968</span><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日出生，西藏自治区贡觉县人，藏族，<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年度“西藏自治区劳动模范”，原嘎玛国际生态文化发展有限公司董事长、西藏天珠之路文化传播有限公司董事长、青海三江源生态环保发展有限公司董事长、东方收藏家协会和自然之友会员等，著名古董商，慈善家，环保人士，中国在押良心犯。长期以来，因其致力于文化与环境保护工作，曾多次获得政府颁发的相关奖项；曾为家乡建桥梁修学校、抚恤孤寡老人；曾成立著名的三江源生态环境保护协会，并从事文物收藏保护；曾创建天珠之路文化传播有限公司，并多次与省级博物馆进行合作；曾与中国藏学研究中心达成协议，准备将<span lang="EN-US">200</span>件珍藏的文物捐献给国家等等，被央视电台提名为<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年度慈善家；本为模范中国公民，之后却因得罪地方当局而备受牢狱之灾。<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年，因其在不知情的前提下购买了总值为<span lang="EN-US">10000</span>美金的七世纪古董毯、刺绣枕垫与鞋子等被盗古墓物品，随被巴州警方以涉嫌“倒卖文物罪”于同年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日刑拘，后经查证其对被窃之物确系毫不知情，且其拥有正规的买卖古董许可证，遂于<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日被取保候审；<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，又因同一罪名被拘，之后又以同一理由于同年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日被取保候审；<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，被正式解除取保候审。但十年之后旧事重提，<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日，第三次因涉嫌“倒卖文物罪”被西藏自治区若羌县警方刑拘，被关押在新疆维吾尔族自治区焉耆回族自治县看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，被正式逮捕；<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，被新疆维吾尔族自治区焉耆回族自治县法院以“盗掘古墓葬罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">15</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">10000</span>元。现在新疆阿克苏地区的沙雅监狱服刑；据悉，在审讯期间曾多次遭遇酷刑，致其左耳几近失聪，双目视力模糊。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">阮晓寰：</span></b><span face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">网名“编程随想”。<span lang="EN-US">1977</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日出生，福建省泉州市人，上海市杨浦区民京路<span lang="EN-US">558</span>号长住居民，网络安全工程师，民主异见人士，中国在押政治犯。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">-2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月间，曾因撰写含有针对中共当局及其政体制度等不利信息的文章百余篇，并将其发布于境外网络平台，在引发网民广泛热议的同时；也引起了中共官方的高度警惕、极端不满和伺机打击；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，因其曾经常使用网名“编程随想”，被中共国安人员查出其在豆瓣网注册过用的个人信息（内含大量针对中共政权的批评性言论），遂被上海市杨浦区警方从家中带走，次日即被以涉嫌“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”刑拘，家遭查抄，当场搜走正在使用中的计算机、手机及多部<span lang="EN-US">/</span>件私人电子设备等物品；同年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被上海市杨浦区检察院以同罪名正式批捕，指控其因长期存有对中共政权的不满情绪，多次“使用计算机编写<span lang="EN-US">100</span>多篇带有造谣、诽谤煽颠性文章，内容涉及攻击抹黑现行政治体制、煽动颠覆国家政权、意图推翻社会主义制度”，并通过境外网站进行发布，造成大量网民浏览、评论、转发和效仿等“恶劣后果”，因而触犯了国家相关法律，应当逮捕法办；在被严重超押近<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，终被上海市第二中级法院一审以“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”秘密重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，剥夺政治权利<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年，没收财产人民币<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日；其不服，上诉；据悉，其被宣判后，其父兄两家均遭警方约谈施压，“劝”其听任政府为其聘用律师，其妻亦遭警察围堵训诫<span lang="EN-US">2</span>小时；截至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，同月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日其案已被上海市高级法院立案，<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，鉴于上海高级法院率先在二审期间使用“法援”律师侵占辩护席位，导致其妻委托律师无法行使合法辩护权，故其家人对相关司法人员的渎职行为和侵犯被告人辩护权等要求彻查纠正，不断信访、举报。目前羁押于上海市杨浦区看守所（上海市杨浦区中原路<span lang="EN-US">1101</span>号，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">200438</span>）。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/03/7_24.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span color="windowtext" face="宋体" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2023/03/7_24.html</span></b></a></span><span face="宋体" lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 12pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">孙文忠、</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">孙秀丽</span><span style="font-family:
