lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，他被逮捕。之后，他被构陷至雁塔区检察院。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月底，宋智被构陷至雁塔区法院。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，雁塔区法院下达判决：宋智被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月。目前，宋智已被劫持到渭南监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/13/%E8%A5%BF%E5%AE%89%E9%9B%81%E5%A1%94%E5%8C%BA%E6%B3%95%E9%99%A2%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E4%BA%8C%E5%8D%81%E5%A4%9A%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98-441220.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/13/%E8%A5%BF%E5%AE%89%E9%9B%81%E5%A1%94%E5%8C%BA%E6%B3%95%E9%99%A2%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E4%BA%8C%E5%8D%81%E5%A4%9A%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98-441220.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">宋志刚：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">辽宁省葫芦岛市兴城市人，兴城市农机修造厂职工，法轮功信仰者，良心犯。因手机丢失，被他人拾到后送到公安局，公安局发现他的手机中存有与法轮功有关的内容，随于<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被新疆阿克陶县公安局拘捕，后被阿克陶县检察院以涉嫌“利用邪教组织破坏法律实施罪”批捕，并被关押在阿克陶县看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月被新疆阿克陶县法院以同罪名枉法重判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">14</span>年，刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2031</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">宋宗孝（宋有福）<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">男，甘肃临夏县新集镇梁家山村法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1941</span>年生。在<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年因写法轮大法标语被抓，被判四年半，在天水监狱遭受迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日（正月初十），临夏县新集派出所警察四人穿着便衣到宋宗孝家骚扰，并撕毁大门上的真相对联。临夏县公安局国保大队伙同新集镇派出所<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月份抓捕了宋宗孝。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月底被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半，并处罚金四千元。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">苏东亮</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">：<span lang="EN-US">1981</span>年出生，前陕西省府谷县法院书记员、民事审判第一庭助审员，维权公民，新公民运动参与者。<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年毕业于西北政法大学之后，<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年，在陕西省府谷县法院参加工作并任书记员；<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年，任民事审判第一庭助理审判员，此期间，一直对现行司法体系的混乱与腐败等问题感到悲凉和无奈，并积极寻求如何改变社会问题的民主之路；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年初，他毅然辞去原有工作，前往广州等地参加民主活动，并与张六毛、项逢选等人结为好友，经常参与围观声援、同城聚餐等活动；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日与张六毛、项逢选等多人一同被广州市珠海区警方以涉“颠覆国家政权罪”刑拘。一个月后被广州天河区检察院以涉“危害国家安全罪”正式批捕，并被定性为“制造炸弹危害公共安全案”主犯之一；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日，获悉与其同案的维权公民张六毛在广州第三看守所被酷刑致死，而依然毫无信息，其家人亦因受官方恐吓而拒绝与外界联系。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月得知，其可能已与项逢选一起被广州市中级法院以“危害国家安全案主犯”判刑。目前服刑监狱不详。刑期不详。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">苏慧丽：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河南省漯河市法轮功学员。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">2022</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，苏慧丽在一学法点被漯河市干河陈派出所警察抓捕；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日遭批捕、<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月被庭审，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚金五千元。苏慧丽已被转监到新乡监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/7/12/462896.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/7/12/462896.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">苏民军：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，山东省籍人，基督徒，北京市灯台基督教家庭教会同工，教会外派差传事工者，中国在押良心犯。因笃信耶稣基督，并积极介入教会服事活动，遂在北京市灯台基督教家庭教会里做同工，后被外派做差传事工人员；因其所在教会属基督教归正福音教会，不愿接受中共自创自办“三自”教会的管辖，遂自新宗教事务条例颁布实施以来，即成为被中共当局欲加逼迫打压的家庭教会之一；其因在信仰倾向上与教会保持鲜明一致，故而亦遭地方政府的监控和伺机打压；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年，苏民军与北京灯台家庭教会秦泗枫牧师一起到云南省开展福音宣教活动，同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，其在宣教事工过程中，被山东省淄博市警方突然跨境抓捕，自此失联；同年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，又被淄博市检察院以涉嫌“非法经营罪”正式批捕，指控其因参与了为教会印制一些敬拜聚会中所使用的赞美诗歌本等行动，遂其言行触犯到中国宗教事务管理条例，故而应予逮捕法办；截至当前，除知其二人各自家属对他们被正式逮捕深表担忧，并迫切呼吁教会信众为其平安获释和坚固信仰的信心而代祷之外，其后续具体情况均不知情。目前被羁押于山东省淄博市看守所（山东省淄博市张店区傅家镇傅家村，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">255063</span>）。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">信息来源：</span></b><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/11/blog-post_96.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/11/blog-post_96.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">隋英华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">辽宁省抚顺法轮功学员。男，一九七二年一月四日出生，清原县清原镇浑河街人，<span lang="EN-US">2000</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日依法去北京为法轮功上访，和几十个法轮功学员在北京的天安门广场打开一条长<span lang="EN-US">99</span>米的巨型横幅，被抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月被北京东城区法院被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年半。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日，隋英华在工作中，被山西省太原市古交派出所五个警察和辽宁省抚顺市清原县河南（腰站）派出所警察抓捕，并抄家，刑事拘留，关押在清原县看守所。后辽宁省抚顺望花区法院法官执法犯法，判清原县法轮功学员隋英华<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">索南次帕（藏）</span></b><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: 宋体; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">西藏昌都地区八宿县人，青年作家，曾在定日县经商。曾因持有达赖喇嘛尊者法像而两次入狱。<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年，索南次帕就曾被冠上“危害国家安全罪”而被判两年徒刑；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，他再次被当局指控“撰写煽动民族矛盾文章、散发达赖喇嘛法像、破坏社会稳定”等，在拉萨遭关押一个月左右，并被处以罚款。索南次帕于<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19&nbsp;</span>日在西藏首都拉萨再次遭当地公安拘捕，这是<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年以来第三次遭到中共公安的拘捕。目前亲友仍不清楚索南次帕被捕的原因，以及关押地点等情况。后音信全无。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">索南公保（藏）：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">1985</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">年出生，四川省甘孜藏族自治州新吧龙县人，藏名<span lang="EN-US">Solnam Gonpo</span>，原甘孜藏族自治州新龙县塘吉乡（音译）小学厨师，藏族人权捍卫者。曾因积极参与罢耕运动和抵制中共控制的藏历新年庆祝活动，<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，被当局怀疑参与在该县塘吉乡（音译）境内的一起有关抗议中共暴政，散发传单、呼吁西藏独立的示威活动；事发当天因该抗议活动引发警民冲突，乡政府办公大楼发生火灾，<span lang="EN-US"> 2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日，随于被新龙县警方强行抓捕，并被以涉嫌“煽动分裂国家罪”和“扰乱社会秩序罪”刑事拘留，关押于四川省成都市某看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2009</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日，被四川省甘孜州中级法院以“煽动分裂国家”和“扰乱社会秩序”两项罪名判处无期徒刑。目前在四川省德阳市黄许镇德阳监狱服刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">索南林珠（藏）：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-size: 11.0pt;">四川甘孜藏区炉霍县人，藏族人权捍卫者。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，在西藏康区炉霍县境内发生大规模和平示威活动后，中共军警釆取武力镇压，导致云丹为首的多名藏人被开枪打死或打伤，上百人遭捕。<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日中共当局对<span lang="EN-US">16</span>名遭捕的藏人进行判决，其中一名藏人被判终身监禁，另有多人遭<span lang="EN-US">1</span>至<span lang="EN-US">13</span>年不等的有期徒刑。这<span lang="EN-US">16</span>名被判藏人中，已确切得知的有<span lang="EN-US">10</span>名藏人具体情况，其中：索南林珠，<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年<span lang="EN-US">30</span>多岁，被判无期徒刑。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">孙百凤：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">河北</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">唐山法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日，唐山市公安局警察抓捕了孙百凤，关押构陷近两年后，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日遭庭审，被判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/3/6/457443.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/3/6/457443.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">孙雪冰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吉林省长春市法轮功学员，男。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日晚上，孙雪冰、王敏夫妻被长春市二道区杨家店派出所抓捕，被关押在兴隆山看守所构陷迫害。王敏被判<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月被劫持到吉林省女子监狱迫害。孙雪冰被判<span lang="EN-US">2</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-size: 11.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/7/24/463365.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/7/24/463365.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">孙策贞：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东青岛法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1956</span>年生，家住青岛市城阳区流亭街道赵村小区。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月份，孙策贞在流亭李家女姑集上告诉百姓法轮大法好的真相时，被便衣绑架。后由家人「取保」回家。在家期间，不断有青岛市即墨区法院人员骚扰、传唤。青岛市即墨区法院要求其和家人及律师到法院开庭。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月份，孙策贞被即墨区法院人员抓捕，开庭。此后，孙策贞被关押至今。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月得知，孙策贞老人被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">孙大骆：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">1957</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年出生，原名孙志明，辽宁省鞍山市人，北京市长驻居民，早期曾为某企业工人和某公司经理，后为北京市某民办学校老师、北京市某残疾人学校校长，职业作家，知名政论作家，民主异见人士，中国在押政治犯。自<span lang="EN-US">1990</span>年代末以来，曾因长期在境外媒体或杂志上发表政论性敏感话题文章，而遭中共当局的关注和严密监控；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年，因在香港与台湾出版《毛泽东权术史》、《习近平权术史》和《当西方哲学压倒中国思想》等多部书籍，并在香港《前哨》和台湾《新纪元》杂志以及境外媒体（如“独立中文笔会”、“北京之春”等）发布政治评论<span lang="EN-US">100</span>余篇，遂于同年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日，被辽宁省沈阳市警方以涉嫌“寻衅滋事罪”刑拘，同时，其家被查抄<span lang="EN-US">5</span>次，其丈母娘家及大姨子家各被抄家<span lang="EN-US">1</span>次；同年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，又被沈阳市经济技术开发区检察院以同罪名予以批捕，并被关押于沈阳市第一看守所；<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日，其案在沈阳市经济技术开发区法院秘密开庭审理，最终被一审以“寻衅滋事罪”判处有期徒刑；因其代理律师及其家属遭警方威胁，不准将其案情向外透露，故其庭审情况、被判日期和被判刑期等讯息，至今鲜为人知。据悉，在看守所被押期间，遭非人道折磨；曾被安排与两个杀人犯关在一起，频遭虐待和殴打，若稍作反抗，就被狱警以违反监规为由戴上重达<span lang="EN-US">10</span>公斤的脚镣；此外，还被禁止说话、看书及购买看守所内食品，并且严禁其向检查组进行申诉；又悉，因其身体健康极差，在看守所时体重不过百斤，患有心脏病和脑血栓，情况堪忧；其妻子王立艳因其被捕亦被当地警方拘留<span lang="EN-US">3</span>天<span lang="EN-US">3</span>夜，受到严厉审讯，使其受到严重惊吓。孙大骆目前在沈阳市某监狱服刑。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/08/blog-post_30.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/08/blog-post_30.html</span></b></a></span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">孙大午：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1954</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月生，河北省徐水县高林村镇郎五庄村人，河北大午农牧集团有限公司董事长。孙大午初中毕业后曾待过山西临汾二十八军八十二师与徐水县农行，这两个经历让他发现农牧业可以发展经营。<span lang="EN-US">1985</span>年他创立大午农牧集团有限公司，担任董事长，以一千只鸡与五十头猪起家。担任董事长期间，孙大午于<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月获颁河北省养鸡状元荣誉。<span lang="EN-US">1995</span>年，大午集团已经成为中国五百大私营企业之一，孙大午也获选为保定市人大代表。<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月，他当选保定市禽蛋产业联合会理事长。<span lang="EN-US">2001</span>年，孙大午除了大午集团董事长外，亦兼任大午学校校长；<span lang="EN-US">2002</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月，他被中国农业大学农民问题研究所聘请为高级研究员。<span lang="EN-US"> 2003</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，徐水县公安局通知大午网站：该网站发表的《小康社会的建设及难点》《悼念李慎之》《两位民间商人关于中国的时局及历史的对话》三篇文章严重损害了国家机关的形象，整顿网站，停止营业<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚款<span lang="EN-US">15000</span>元。<span lang="EN-US"> 2003</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，他被指向三千多户农民借款达一亿八千多万元而被捕，并以非法集资的罪名遭到收押，并被指控其非法持有弹药；两位弟弟大午集团副董事长孙志华、总经理孙德华和集团的财务处长也都被扣留。最终徐水县法院以非法吸收公众存款的罪名判其有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年、缓刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">10</span>万元，大午集团同时也被判处罚金三十万元。于<span lang="EN-US">2003</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日出狱回家。孙大午于<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日被河北高碑店市公安局刑事拘留，指控他涉嫌寻衅滋事罪和破坏生产经营。同时，其妻子、两个儿子儿媳、公司高管等<span lang="EN-US">28</span>人一并被抓捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，河北大午集团此前被“指定居所监视居住”的<span lang="EN-US">7</span>位当事人家属，分别收到公安送达的逮捕通知书。孙大午被控<span lang="EN-US">8</span>项罪名，分别是：非法吸收公众存款罪、寻衅滋事罪、非法采矿罪、聚众冲击国家机关罪、非法占用农用地罪、强迫交易罪、破坏生产经营罪、妨害公务罪。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日<span lang="EN-US">9</span>时至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日<span lang="EN-US">16</span>时，大午案经历<span lang="EN-US">14</span>天庭审后当庭宣判：大午农牧集团有限公司：罚金<span lang="EN-US">3050</span>万元，依法追缴违法所得<span lang="EN-US">1447.54</span>万元，责令大午农牧集团有限公司退赔非法集资款项人民币<span lang="EN-US">10.37</span>亿元。孙大午被判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">18</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">311</span>万元；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2038</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">孙德华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">大午集团副监事长，孙大午二弟。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日凌晨，河北大午农牧集团负责人孙大午及其亲属并集团子公司法人等近<span lang="EN-US">30</span>人被警方突击抓捕。其后，包括孙大午妻子刘会茹等部分公司高管，被以“非法吸收公众存款”罪名批捕，而孙大午等其他公司高管以“指定居所监视居住”的方式被采取强制措施。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，河北大午集团此前被“指定居所监视居住”的<span lang="EN-US">7</span>位当事人家属，分别收到公安送达的逮捕通知书。孙德华被控罪名：非法吸收公众存款罪、寻衅滋事罪、非法采矿罪、聚众冲击国家机关罪、非法占用农用地罪、强迫交易罪、破坏生产经营罪、妨害公务罪。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日<span lang="EN-US">9</span>时至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日<span lang="EN-US">16</span>时，大午案经历<span lang="EN-US">14</span>天庭审后当庭宣判：孙德华被判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">190</span>万元；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2032</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormalCxSpMiddle"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">孙德香：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">女，<span lang="EN-US">1956</span>年生，黑龙江省伊春市法轮功</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">五营区</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">学员。<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，中共开始疯狂迫害法轮功，孙德香遭中共邪党人员抓捕、关押，<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日曾经被判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月初，孙德香被伊春市公安局恶警秘密抓捕。孙德香后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，现已被关押在黑龙江省女子监狱。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月获悉</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">孙德香现在身体被迫害得很严重，被转到黑龙江省监狱管理局中心医院，说是肠癌，家属被告知交钱并签字，是给孙德香做手术。</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月初。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormalCxSpMiddle"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/5/25/-%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%BA%94%E6%9C%88%E4%BA%8C%E5%8D%81%E4%BA%94%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-444055.html#22524234855-1"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/5/25/-%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%BA%94%E6%9C%88%E4%BA%8C%E5%8D%81%E4%BA%94%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-444055.html#22524234855-1</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormalCxSpMiddle" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-add-space: auto; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">孙鼎美：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">女，山东烟台法轮功学员。</span><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">2021</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日，烟台市莱山区公安局有预谋的绑架了十几名法轮功学员，关押在烟台市福山看守所。其中张美玲、孙鼎美遭受八个月的关押、构陷后，被判刑，张美玲被判<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚款<span lang="EN-US">6000</span>元；孙鼎美<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，罚款<span lang="EN-US">5000</span>元。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月初宣判后，张美玲、孙鼎美上诉烟台市中级法院。烟台市中级法院二审维持原判。孙鼎美刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/5/27/2022-5-27.html#22526225225-2"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/5/27/2022-5-27.html#22526225225-2</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">孙广利：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">黑龙江省齐齐哈尔市法轮功学员。孙广利、孟素英夫妇，黑龙江省齐齐哈尔市碾子山区人，暂住辽宁省沈阳市。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">6</span>日晚<span lang="EN-US">7</span>点多孙广利、孟素英夫妇，在沈阳市辽中区<span lang="EN-US">6</span>间房镇的<span lang="EN-US">1</span>个村子里发了几张告诉世人如何躲避瘟疫的方法，被人诬告，<span lang="EN-US">6</span>间房派出所的警察将<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人抓捕到当地派出所进行关押。 由于那时中国疫情严重，看守所不接收，次日晚<span lang="EN-US">7</span>点多将<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人放回家中。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日晚<span lang="EN-US">7</span>点左右，东街派出所的<span lang="EN-US">5</span>、<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个警察又到家中将夫妻<span lang="EN-US">2</span>人强行抓捕到东街派出所。<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日晚，丈夫孙广利被关押到沈阳第二看守所，妻子孟素英被关押到沈阳第一看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日傍晚，他们的家人接到法院通知：孙广利、孟素英夫妇判决已下来，最终两人均被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">孙桂昌：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">吉林省德惠市五台乡法轮功学员。孙桂昌和肖永芬夫妇各被非法判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年，已经于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月份被羁押到公主岭监狱和吉林省女子监狱。孙桂昌和妻子肖永芬<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日被不法警察入室绑架。孙贵昌被送到德惠市拘留所非法拘留五天。肖永芬被送到长春第二看守所检查身体，不合格拒收，第二天下午<span lang="EN-US">7</span>点多钟放回家，被监视居住。后来，孙桂昌被非法关押德惠看守所。肖永芬因身体和精神状况被放回家，并被监视居住。<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日左右，吉林省公安厅数个警察将在其女儿看家的肖永芬绑架。据悉，肖永芬以前在长春黑嘴子劳教所被迫害得精神失常，现在患有高血压和糖尿病（后期），脚部严重溃烂，现在被关押在吉林省女子监狱八监区；孙桂昌被关押在公主岭监狱九监区。多年来，上述两个监狱公开执法犯法，利用死人床、坐小板凳、长期剥夺睡眠、电棍电击、殴打、上绳等各种酷刑残害和转化善良无辜的法轮功学员，多人被迫害致伤、致残、致疯、致死。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">孙继萍</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：辽宁锦州凌海市法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">68</span>岁。在中共对法轮功的迫害中，孙继萍与丈夫周永林被中共绑架、关押，劳教，在派出所、看守所、劳教所遭酷刑折磨。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，孙继萍与丈夫周永林在盘锦市锦采新区大集上告诉人们“法轮大法好”时，被凌海市公安局闫家镇派出所警察绑架，被隔离二十一天后（<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日），孙继萍被非法关押到锦州市女子看守所，周永林被非法关押到凌海市看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月，凌海市法院对孙继萍与丈夫周永林每人各判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年、罚金各一万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">孙建锋</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：宁夏中卫市中宁县法轮功学员。自<span lang="EN-US">1999</span>年中共对法轮功持续至今已逾二十多年的迫害中，<span lang="EN-US">1972</span>年生的孙建锋先生曾经被劳教<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年半、判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日晚，孙建锋先生被一小区的保安诬告，警察将孙建锋绑架后搜身，并闯入孙建锋家抄家，劫掠了两本大法书籍，随后将孙建锋劫持到中宁县看守所关押，后孙建锋被批捕。孙建锋先生<span lang="EN-US">2010</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日被判<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>个月。孙建锋已经被关押到宁夏石嘴山监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">湖北荆州法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日下午<span lang="EN-US">5</span>点多钟，丈夫李行军从母亲家出来，刚下楼，就被国保、西门派出所警察、学校保卫科等多人抓捕，他们对他拳打脚踢，打的满脸是血。被强行带上警车后，就送到西门看守所去了。妻子孙江怡也被抓走。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日才开庭。李行军、孙江怡夫妇被庭审，两人都被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日发送法轮功台历，被泰山区公安分局抓捕，遭泰山区检察院构陷，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年七月二十日被泰山区法院开庭，被判<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>个月，罚金两万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">9</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">辽宁省新宾县法轮功学员，<span lang="EN-US">1954</span>年生，女。孙静是<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日晚<span lang="EN-US">7</span>点左右，在家被抚顺市新宾县国保队长张立军带领刑警、新宾镇派出所警察十多人抓捕的。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>十<span lang="EN-US">1</span>日，辽宁省新宾县孙静在抚顺看守所被开庭，<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日，法院人员通知家属孙静被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。孙静于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日被转入到辽宁女子监狱服刑。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">孙晶：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">又名孙静，女，<span lang="EN-US">1970</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日出生于丹东，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年开始修炼法轮功的学员，家住抚顺市将军地区。孙晶的丈夫胡国舰因为修炼法轮功，曾两遭冤狱，<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年，被中共迫害致死。孙晶深受刺激，心身疲惫，健康出现危机。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年，她有缘开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">21</span>日，孙晶和王秀国，因在抚顺市顺城区前甸镇附近给民众介“法轮功，被顺城区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，各被罚金五千元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/3/28/458206.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">孙利：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河北省唐山市法轮功学员，男，原唐山钢铁公司职工。因修炼法轮功，曾被劳教、判刑迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">31</span>日，河北唐山市东窑派出所警察，在一位老年法轮功学员家，抓捕了孙利。孙利被关押在唐山市第一看守所。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日在路北区法院被庭审，后被判刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">孙丽华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">辽宁省鞍山市大法学员。孙丽华在<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年上半年坐火车去锦州办事，身上带的法轮功材料，被乘警发现，在锦州被拘留<span lang="EN-US">5</span>天。在<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，孙丽华去铁东公安分局办理解除“监视居住”手续时，被扣留。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，孙丽华被逮捕，<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日下午，孙丽华庭审。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">8</span>日，孙丽华再次被开庭。最后，孙丽华被判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<u><span lang="EN-US">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2022/9/24/450015.html<o:p></o:p></span></u></b></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">孙丽娟：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">辽宁省锦州市法轮功学员，女。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日，河南省焦作市公安局解放区分局国保大队及锦州市公安局凌河区分局国保大队和锦州市菊园派出所二十余人，闯入孙丽娟家中抄家，并抓捕了孙丽娟和她丈夫张宝国。张宝国被劫持到锦州看守所，关押三十七天后，以“取保候审”的形式回家。孙丽娟被关押在锦州市女子看守所。据悉，孙丽娟因在网上利用微信向民众讲法轮功，被河南省焦作市国保大队监控到。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月，孙丽娟被凌海市检察院批捕。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月，凌海市检察院对孙丽娟提起公诉，将孙丽娟的所谓“卷宗”交到了凌海市法院。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月被锦州市凌海法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罚金一万元，上诉被锦州市中级法院维持原判。据悉，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日，孙丽娟被关押到辽宁省女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/4/26/459216.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/4/26/459216.html</span></b></a></span><b><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; lang="EN-US">11</span>日凌晨，河北大午农牧集团负责人孙大午及其亲属并集团子公司法人等近<span lang="EN-US">30</span>人被警方突击抓捕。其后，包括孙大午妻子刘会茹等部分公司高管，被以“非法吸收公众存款”罪名批捕，而孙大午等其他公司高管以“指定居所监视居住”的方式被采取强制措施。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，河北大午集团此前被“指定居所监视居住”的<span lang="EN-US">7</span>位当事人家属，分别收到公安送达的逮捕通知书。孙萌被控罪名：非法吸收公众存款罪、非法占用农用地罪、非法采矿罪、强迫交易罪、诈骗罪。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">16</span>时，大午案经历<span lang="EN-US">14</span>天庭审后当庭宣判：孙萌被判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">12</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">190</span>万元；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2032</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">27</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">孙清：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">青海省海东市互助土族自治县人，网络活跃人士，推特账号<span lang="EN-US">@maowus2</span>、<span lang="EN-US">@ruoguang86 </span>、<span lang="EN-US">@cittakusala</span>注册者，社会时政关注者，民主宪政追求者，中国在押政治犯。自<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年以来，因关注社会时政而经常在微信和推特等国内外网络平台发布或转发对中共当局施政政策及手段等的批评性文图信息，遂遭青海省当局严控打压；<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月，曾翻防火墙注册推特账号<span lang="EN-US">@maowus2</span>，多次发布对中共政府不利的负面信息；<span lang="EN-US">2015</span>年，又在国内网络上注册微信账号，在微信群里十数次发表对中共政治制度的批评性言论，故而遭到互助县警方的严密监控；<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月和<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月，曾因再次分别注册两个推特账号<span lang="EN-US">@ruoguang86 </span>、<span lang="EN-US">@cittakusala</span>，并由此利用其三个推特账号交替发布了数千条揭批中共当局及其高层领导人、对新冠防疫政策与措施的不合理制定及滥用，以及中共当局对民族政策采取高压严管手段等信息，遂引发社会广泛热议；据悉，其在推特上曾因累计发布<span lang="EN-US">7703</span>条敏感信息，故而赢得网友点赞<span lang="EN-US">2.1</span>万余次，其中推特账号<span lang="EN-US">@ruoguang86</span>被关注者共计<span lang="EN-US">1965</span>名，同时，其在微信朋友圈中亦因累计发送<span lang="EN-US">106</span>条对政府声望不利的负面信息，好友人数多达<span lang="EN-US">616</span>名，遂很快引起青海省当局的极大恐惧和报复性打压；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月，青海省公安厅国保总队组成项目组，责令互助土族自治县警方对其立即实施抓捕、刑拘，涉嫌罪名疑是“煽动颠覆国家政权罪”等；后其被互助土族自治县检察院以同罪名正式批捕，指控其因在<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年<span lang="EN-US">-2019</span>年期间，多次在微信朋友圈和推特上发布“攻击中国社会主义制度、污蔑党和国家领导人、诋毁疫情防控工作、危害国家和领土主权完整以及破坏民族团结等有害信息”，遂应予以逮捕判刑；<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月，其案在青海省互助土族自治县法院开庭审理，至今尚未宣判。目前被羁押于青海省互助县看守所（青海省海东市互助土族自治县，邮政编码：<span lang="EN-US">810500</span>）。<b>信息来源：<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/12/blog-post_26.html"><b><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://wqw2010.blogspot.com/2022/12/blog-post_26.html</span></b></a></span><b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">孙润桃：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">河北省张家口市沽源县法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">17</span>日下午，沽源县法轮功学员高清秀、孙润桃、赵梅在长梁乡顺路讲法轮功、免费传递法轮功法轮功资料时，遭人恶告，遭警方抓捕。孙润桃和高清秀<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日，分别被张北县法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年和<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年，勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">2</span>万元。孙润桃刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">8</span>月<span lang="EN-US">16</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">孙茜：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">加拿大华裔女富商。孙茜是北京利德曼生物化学公司的创始人，<span lang="EN-US">2007</span>年获加拿大国籍，<span lang="EN-US">2012</span>年和<span lang="EN-US">2016</span>年登上胡润中国富豪榜，身家<span lang="EN-US">35</span>亿。由于操劳过度，身体严重透支，孙茜患上多种疾病，多方医治无效。在<span lang="EN-US">2014</span>年她学习炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2017</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日，孙茜正在家中与表妹聊天，警方突然闯入抄家，搜出法轮功相关书籍后，将她抓捕。期间，孙茜多次遭受酷刑，被铐在铁椅子上，被辣椒水喷脸。全天被戴上镣铐，强制洗脑，强迫放弃她的信仰。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">30</span>日，孙茜一案在北京朝阳法院温榆河法庭开庭，孙茜获刑<span lang="EN-US">8</span>年。刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-font-family: Calibri; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-latin; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-font-family: Calibri; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-latin;">孙士伟：</span></b><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1953</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年生，黑龙江穆棱市教师进修学校美术教研员，法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2005</span>年，孙士伟因在一次歌会上为了表达对大法师父的敬仰，唱了一首大法弟子创作的歌曲，被人举报，九月二十三日被警察突然闯入家中绑架，遭毒打折磨，<span lang="EN-US">2006</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月被判刑八年，在佳木斯莲江口监狱遭受了种种迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日下午，穆棱市建行小区的一位老人曹淑芳家中的玻璃碎了，孙士伟、高朋光、高永丽三人帮其修理。国保警察突然出现抓捕了孙士伟、高朋光、高永丽三人，并抄了三人的家。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，海林市法院下判决，高永丽被诬判<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>个月，高朋光和孙士伟被诬判<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，分别处以两万罚金。孙士伟刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">孙淑杰：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">黑龙江省双鸭山市尖山区法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年六十五岁。原是双鸭山矿业集团公司林业处森保站站长兼任生产技术科副科长。一九九六年七月修炼法轮功。曾十四次被抓捕迫害，遭五年冤狱，回来不久，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">23</span>日又被抓捕、构陷，又被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，目前已经被关押到黑龙江省女子监狱。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span><span href="http://4.31.18.88/mh/articles/2022/3/19/%E6%9B%BE%E9%81%AD%E5%8D%81%E5%A4%9A%E5%B9%B4%E7%89%A2%E7%8B%B1%E8%BF%AB%E5%AE%B3-%E9%BB%91%E9%BE%99%E6%B1%9F%E5%AD%99%E6%B7%91%E6%9D%B0%E5%8F%88%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E5%9B%9B%E5%B9%B4-440225.html"><b lang="EN-US">4</span>日，孙淑霞和董宇在长春市南关区平泉路附近发放法轮功资料，被长春市公安局南关分局曙光路派出所警察抓捕。当日被抄家，将孙淑霞、董宇劫持到长春市苇子沟看守所关押迫害。后因疫情原因，一个月后，孙淑霞、董宇被所谓“监视居住”。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日，孙淑霞、董宇又被抓捕、关押。长春市公检法人员相互勾结，利用刑法<span lang="EN-US">300</span>条所谓“破坏法律实施”的罪名对孙淑霞、董宇进行迫害。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月中旬获悉：孙淑霞被长春市朝阳区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a lang="EN-US">1970</span>年生，哈尔滨市宾县宁远镇爱国村王油坊屯人。一九九五年，孙太荣开始修炼法轮功。孙太荣女士因告诉租户避疫良方遭恶告，于<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日被警察抓捕，<span minor-fareast;">退休工人，家住辽宁省抚顺市东洲区。她从<span lang="EN-US">1996</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月开始修炼法轮功。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>月初得知，孙文稳老人在流离失所期间被抓捕，<span minor-fareast;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">孙秀丽：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"> 广州法轮功学员，女，<span lang="EN-US">1973</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月出生，黑龙江省肇东市人，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">3</span>日因制作和发放法轮功资料在广州被抓捕。她被抓捕前在广州市天河区火锅店打工。广州市海珠区法院<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月对孙秀丽判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚金一万五千元；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">2</span>日<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">。信息来源：</b></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/4/21/459037.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/4/21/459037.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; tab-stops: 122.5pt; text-align: left;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">孙秀英</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">：吉林农安县法轮功学员。女、<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">68</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，长春市农安县抓捕了<span lang="EN-US">20</span>多名法轮功学员。此次抓捕行动，是由长春市政法委和农安县政法委共同策划实施的。此次被抓捕的法轮功学员有</span><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">张秀芝、高晓歧、蔡玉英、吴冬梅、于姣茹、单为和、赵秀兰、孙秀英、张敬元、孙凤仙、冯立齐、吕相富、董秀辉等<span lang="EN-US" style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">22</span><span style="mso-bidi-font-weight: bold;">名法轮功学员被抓捕。他们被抓捕、构陷<span lang="EN-US">1</span>年多后，有十几名法轮功学员被德惠市法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">2</span>至<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年。其中：孙秀英被判<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万；刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日。<b>信息来源：</b></span></span><span lang="EN-US"><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/5/%E5%90%89%E6%9E%9713%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E4%BA%8C%E5%88%B0%E5%8D%81%E5%B9%B4-%E4%B8%AD%E6%B3%95%E7%BB%B4%E6%8C%81%E5%86%A4%E5%88%A4-434381.html"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2021/12/5/%E5%90%89%E6%9E%9713%E5%90%8D%E6%B3%95%E8%BD%AE%E5%8A%9F%E5%AD%A6%E5%91%98%E8%A2%AB%E6%9E%89%E5%88%A4%E4%BA%8C%E5%88%B0%E5%8D%81%E5%B9%B4-%E4%B8%AD%E6%B3%95%E7%BB%B4%E6%8C%81%E5%86%A4%E5%88%A4-434381.html</span></b></a></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><a name="_Hlk52322719"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">孙永耀：</span></b></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk52322719;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">1970</span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk52322719;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日出生，安徽省阜南县人，阜南县鹿城镇刘寨村孙西组<span lang="EN-US">13</span>号公民，基督徒，安徽省阜南县基督教堂主任牧师，中国在押良心犯。<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月，其所在教会接到当地政府发来的要求拆除教堂通知，称其教堂因地处政府要进行街道棚改项目改造规划的范畴，故而必须拆除；由于地方当局仅对其所在教会提出单方面拆迁补偿方案，并称如要教堂异地重建，政府将不给予相应补偿；因此通告方案明显有失公允，立刻遭到其及教会众信徒的坚决反对，遂遭地方当局的恶意报复与打击；<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，正当众信徒在教会举行聚会和敬拜时，突然被官方拆迁公司闯入，并在无任何合法档及拆除手续的情况下实施强拆，因事发突然，教会里面的所有物品均未及时搬出，终致所有财物几近损毁；因其坚决反对政府强拆教堂的举动，同年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">18</span>日，遂与教会主任耿宜敏等神职人员一同被阜南市警方抓捕，次日被以涉“聚众扰乱社会秩序罪”刑拘；<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk52322719;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">同年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，被阜阳县检察院予以批捕；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">29</span>日，其案在安徽省阜南县法院开庭受审；<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日，被该法院一审以“聚众扰乱社会秩序罪”判处有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月；其不服，提起上诉；<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">12</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日，安徽省阜阳市中级法院经二审裁决，认为“原判认定的部分事实不清，证据不足”，故撤销原判，发回重审。目前被羁押于阜南县看守所。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 106%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk52322719;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">孙玉斌：</span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk52322719;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">山东聊城市七旬法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">74</span>岁，山东聊城水城集团退休，修炼法轮功后，身心受益。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">13</span>日，孙玉斌在聊城财干路贴法轮功不干胶时，遭东昌府区香江派出所抓捕。警察晚<span lang="EN-US">7</span>点抄他家，抢走了大法书、电脑等。孙玉斌被关押在茌平区看守所构陷。关押半年，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月初被聊城市东阿县法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年、勒索罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万元。因中共肺炎的原因，他还被关押在聊城看守所。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">12</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/4/15/%E5%B1%B1%E4%B8%9C%E8%81%8A%E5%9F%8E%E5%B8%82%E4%B8%83%E6%97%AC%E5%AD%99%E7%8E%89%E6%96%8C%E8%A2%AB%E9%9D%9E%E6%B3%95%E5%88%A4%E5%88%91%E4%B8%89%E5%B9%B4-441291.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk52322719;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: _Hlk52322719;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;">孙煜山：</span></b></span><span 0pt;">长沙市青年法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">1998</span>年生，<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年年仅<span lang="EN-US">25</span>岁。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月<span lang="EN-US">20</span>日被长沙市清水塘派出所抄家、抓捕，<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">7</span>日被构陷至浏阳市法院。<span lang="EN-US">2023</span>年<span lang="EN-US">2</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日，他被开庭判刑<span lang="EN-US">3</span>年<span lang="EN-US">3</span>个月、勒索一万多罚金。目前，孙煜山在长沙市第二看守所羁押。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2025</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">19</span>日<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">。信息来源：</b></span></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/2/18/456895.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk52322719;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">孙玉霞<span lang="EN-US">:</span></span></b></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk52322719;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;"> </span></span><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk52322719;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">山东省东营市胜利油田河口区法轮功学员。范志勇、孙玉霞法轮功夫妇于<span lang="EN-US">2013</span>年七月曾因制作发放神韵光盘，被山东滨州沾化法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">6</span>年，孙玉霞被判缓刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。范志勇于<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年出狱后，被单位开除，失去了生活经济来源，为了生活和孙玉霞走到一起，开办“小饭桌”维持生计。范志勇、孙玉霞夫妇<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">5</span>月<span lang="EN-US">5</span>日被警察被抓捕，日前被东营区法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年，罚款两万元；孙玉霞被判刑<span lang="EN-US">4</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>个月，罚款<span lang="EN-US">1</span>万六千元。孙玉霞刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2026</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">4</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：</b></span></span><a href="https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/1/8/454651.html"><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk52322719;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="color: windowtext; font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-font-kerning: 0pt; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">https://www.minghui.org/mmh/articles/2023/1/8/454651.html</span></b></span></a><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk52322719;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 106%; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></b></span></p><span style="mso-bookmark: _Hlk52322719;"></span><p class="MsoNormal"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">孙占国：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">吉林省松原市干安县法轮功学员。家住松原市干安县唱子村，在中共对法轮功的疯狂迫害中，孙占国曾连续两次被非法劳教，曾被关押在吉林省九台饮马河劳教所，遭受酷刑虐待。<span lang="EN-US">2019</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月被干安县油田采油厂派出所抓捕，被关押一年后，<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月被干安县法院判刑<span lang="EN-US">5</span>年。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2024</span>年<span lang="EN-US">9</span>月。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">孙志芬</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">：山西太原市老年法轮功学员。太原市公安局迎泽分局警察<span lang="EN-US">2018</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日非法闯民宅，抄家抓捕法轮功学员孙志芬（<span lang="EN-US">60</span>岁）、王素平（<span lang="EN-US">67</span>岁）、罗保军（<span lang="EN-US">62</span>岁）、张清香（<span lang="EN-US">69</span>岁）、张润英（<span lang="EN-US">71</span>岁）、郭润鲜（<span lang="EN-US">68</span>岁）、田玉琴（<span lang="EN-US">60</span>岁）、胡兰英（<span lang="EN-US">65</span>岁），其中多数是老太太。山西省太原市这八位老年法轮功学员被非法关押近一年后得知被迎泽区法院非法判刑、勒索罚款，并被劫持到监狱。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;;">被判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年，罚金<span lang="EN-US">3</span>万元。刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2028</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">24</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p class="MsoNormal" style="tab-stops: 141.95pt;"><b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">孙志华：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; mso-ascii-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-bidi-font-weight: bold; mso-fareast-font-family: 宋体; mso-fareast-theme-font: minor-fareast; mso-hansi-theme-font: minor-fareast;">大午集团副监事长，孙大午亲属。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">11</span>日凌晨，河北大午农牧集团负责人孙大午及其亲属并集团子公司法人等近<span lang="EN-US">30</span>人被警方突击抓捕。其后，包括孙大午妻子刘会茹等部分公司高管，被以“非法吸收公众存款”罪名批捕，而孙大午等其他公司高管以“指定居所监视居住”的方式被采取强制措施。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">4</span>月<span lang="EN-US">22</span>日，河北大午集团此前被“指定居所监视居住”的<span lang="EN-US">7</span>位当事人家属，分别收到公安送达的逮捕通知书。孙志华被控罪名：寻衅滋事罪、非法采矿罪、聚众冲击国家机关罪、非法占用农用地罪、破坏生产经营罪、妨害公务罪。<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">15</span>日<span lang="EN-US">9</span>时至<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">7</span>月<span lang="EN-US">28</span>日<span lang="EN-US">16</span>时，大午案经历<span lang="EN-US">14</span>天庭审后当庭宣判：孙志华被判有期徒刑<span lang="EN-US">9</span>年，并处罚金<span lang="EN-US">55</span>万元；刑期至<span lang="EN-US">2029</span>年<span lang="EN-US">11</span>月<span lang="EN-US">10</span>日。<span lang="EN-US"><o:p></o:p></span></span></p><p align="left" class="MsoNormal" style="line-height: 107%; margin-bottom: 8.0pt; mso-pagination: widow-orphan; text-align: left;"><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%;">孙中丽：</span></b><span style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%;">辽宁省大连市法轮功学员。<span lang="EN-US">2020</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">26</span>日，大连市法轮功学员任海飞在自己所租住的钻石湾寓所，被大连市公安局甘井子区分局国保大队和甘井子街派出所警察抓捕并抄家，抢走逾<span lang="EN-US">55</span>万元现金，以及价值<span lang="EN-US">20</span>多万元的存储卡等电子产品。孙中丽同时被抓捕。任海飞、孙中丽被关押构陷一年多后，于<span lang="EN-US">2021</span>年<span lang="EN-US">10</span>月<span lang="EN-US">14</span>日宣判，任海飞被判刑<span lang="EN-US">10</span>年并罚款十万元。孙中丽被判刑<span lang="EN-US">7</span>年、罚款七万元。他们都已上诉。<span lang="EN-US">2022</span>年<span lang="EN-US">1</span>月初被告知，不开庭维持原判。孙中丽刑期至：<span lang="EN-US">2027</span>年<span lang="EN-US">6</span>月<span lang="EN-US">25</span>日。<b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;">信息来源：<u><span lang="EN-US">https://www.minghui.org/mh/articles/2022/1/17/%E4%BA%8C%E9%9B%B6%E4%BA%8C%E4%BA%8C%E5%B9%B4%E4%B8%80%E6%9C%88%E5%8D%81%E4%B8%83%E6%97%A5%E5%A4%A7%E9%99%86%E7%BB%BC%E5%90%88%E6%B6%88%E6%81%AF-436935.html</span></u></b></span><b style="mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;"><u><span lang="EN-US" style="font-family: 宋体; font-size: 12.0pt; line-height: 107%; mso-bidi-font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; mso-font-kerning: 0pt;"><o:p></o:p></span></u></b></p><br /><p></p>
</div>
